interference\n115\t\t\tcombinedAmp := directAmp + reflAmp*math.Cos(directPhase-reflPhase)\n116\t\t\tcombinedPhase := 1.0\n128\t\t}\n129\t\n130\t\t// Normalize phase\n131\t\tif weight > 0 {\n132\t\t\ttotalPhase /= weight\n133\t\t}\n134\t\n135\t\treturn totalAmplitude, totalPhase\n136\t}\n137\t\n138\t// computeDirectPath computes the CSI contribution from the direct path\n139\t// through the walker to the receiver, using the log-distance path loss model.\n140\tfunc computeDirectPath(tx, rx, walker Point, walls []Wall) (float64, float64) {\n141\t\t// Distance from TX to walker\n142\t\td1 := distance(tx, walker)\n143\t\t// Distance from walker to RX\n144\t\td2 := distance(walker, rx)\n145\t\t// zone calculation\n152\t\texcess := dTotal - dDirect\n153\t\tif excess < 0 {\n154\t\t\texcess = 0\n155\t\t}\n156\t\n157\t\t// Fresnel zone number\n158\t\tzoneNumber := int(math.Ceil(excess / halfWavelength))\n159\t\tif zoneNumber < 1 {\n160\t\t\tzoneNumber = 1\n161\t\t}\n162\t\n163\t\t// Zone decay (inverse square)\n164\t\tdecay := 1.0 / math.Pow(float64(zoneNumber), 2.0)\n165\t\n166\t\t// Log-distance path loss model: PL(d) = PL_0 + 10*n*log10(d/d_0)\n167\t\tvar pathLossDB float64\n168\t\tif dTotal >= d0 {\n169\t\t\tpathLossDB = pl0 + path\n176\t\twallLoss := computeWallLoss(tx, walker, walls)\n177\t\twallLoss += computeWallLoss(walker, rx, walls)\n178\t\n179\t\t// Total loss in dB\n180\t\ttotalLossDB := pathLossDB + wallLoss\n181\t\n182\t\t// Convert to linear amplitude\n183\t\tamplitude := math.Pow(10.0, -totalLossDB/20.0)\n184\t\n185\t\t// Apply Fresnel zone decay\n186\t\tamplitude *= decay\n187\t\n188\t\t// Phase at this position (based on total path length)\n189\t\tphase := 2 * math.Pi * dTotal / wavelength\n190\t\n191\t\treturn amplitude, phase\n192\t}\n193\t\n194\t// computeFirstOrderReflection Uses image method to find reflection point.\n196\tfunc computeFirstOrderReflection(tx, rx, walker Point, walls []Wall) (float64, float64) {\n197\t\tvar bestReflAmp float64\n198\t\tvar bestReflPhase {\n253\t\t\treturn 0, 0\n254\t\t}\n255\t\n256\t\treturn bestReflAmp, bestReflPhase\n257\t}\n258\t\n259\t// findReflectionPoint finds the specular reflection point on a wall segment\n260\t// for a ray from TX to RX using the image method.\n261\t// Returns the reflection point and true if a valid reflection exists, false otherwise.\n262\tfunc findReflectionPoint(tx, rx Point, wall Wall) (Point, {\n518\t\t\ti = 127\n519\t\t}\n520\t\tif i < -127 {\n521\t\t\ti = -127\n522\t\t}\n523\t\tif q > 127 {\n524\t\t\tq = 127\n525\t\t}\n526\t\tif q < -127 {\n527\t\t\tq = / 2.0\n\tsubcarrierSpacing = 312.5e3 // Hz\n\tc                 = 3e8     // speed of light m/s\n\n\t// CSI frame constants — must match ingestion/frame.go format\n\tnSub = 64 // number of subcarriers for HT20\n\n\t// Path loss model constants (log-distance model)\n\t// PL(d) = PL_0 + 10*n*log10(d/d_0)\n\tpl0    = 40.0 // dBm reference power at d0\n\td0     = 1.0   // meters reference distance\n\tn frame format matches the ingestion layer (ingestion/frame.go):\n//\n//\tHeader (24 bytes fixed):\n//\t  [0:6]   node_mac     — TX node MAC address\n//\t  [6:12]  peer_mac     — RX node MAC address\n//\t  [12:20] timestamp_us — uint64 LE, microseconds since node boot\n//\t  [20]    rssi         — int8, dBm\n//\t  [21]    noise_floor  — int8, dBm\n//\t  [22]    channel      — uint8, WiFi channel\n//\t  [23]    n_sub        — uint8, subcarrier count\n//\tPayload (n_sub × 2 bytes):\n//\t  Per subcarrier: int8 I, int8 Q\nfunc generateCSIFrame(tx, rx *VirtualNode, walkers []*Walker, walls []Wall, frameNum int, rng *rand.Rand) []byte {\n\t// Calculate combined CSI from all walkers\n\tamplitude, phaseBase := computeCSIForWalkers(tx, rx, walkers, walls)\n\n\t// Compute RSSI from amplitude\n\trssi := amplitudeToRSSI(amplitude)\n\n\t// Create frame buffer (headerSize=24 defined in main.go)\n\tframe := make([]byte, headerSize+nSub*2)\n\n\t// Write header (matches ingestion/frame.go ParseFrame layout)\n\tcopy(frame[0:6], tx.MAC[:])   // node_mac\n\tcopy(frame[6:12], rx.MAC[:])  // peer_mac\n\tbinary.LittleEndian.PutUint64(frame[12:20], uint64(frameNum*50000)) // timestamp_us\n\tframe[20] = byte(rssi)        // rssi\n\tvar noiseFloor int8 = -95\n\tframe[21] = byte(noiseFloor) // noise_floor: -95 dBm\n\tframe[22] = byte(*flagChannel) // channel (from --channel flag)\n\tframe[23] = nSub              // n_sub\n\n\t// Generate I/Q pairs for each subcarrier\n\tfor k := 0; k < nSub; k++ {\n\t\t// Phase for this subcarrier\n\t\tphase := phaseBase + float64(k)*0.1\n\n\t\t// Add temporal variation\n\t\tphase += 0.1 * math.Sin(2*math.Pi*float64(frameNum)/100.0)\n\n\t\t// Normalize phase to [-π, π]\n\t\tfor phase > math.Pi {\n\t\t\tphase -= 2 * math.Pi\n\t\t}\n\t\tfor phase < -math.Pi {\n\t\t\tphase += 2 * math.Pi\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Add frequency-selective fading\n\t\tfreqFading := 0.8 + 0.4*math.Sin(2*math.Pi*float64(k)/16.0)\n\t\tsubAmplitude := amplitude * freqFading\n\n\t\t// Generate I/Q with noise\n\t\ti, q := generateIQPair(subAmplitude, phase, rng)\n\n\t\t// Write to payload (interleaved I,Q)\n\t\toffset := headerSize + k*2\n\t\tframe[offset] = byte(i)\n\t\tframe[offset+1] = byte(q)\n\t}\n\n\treturn frame\n}\n\n// computeCSIForWalkers computes the combined CSI amplitude and phase from all walkers\n// using a two-ray propagation model (direct path + first-order reflection).\nfunc computeCSIForWalkers(tx, rx *VirtualNode, walkers []*Walker, walls []Wall) (float64, float64) {\n\tif len(walkers) == 0 {\n\t\t// No walkers, return baseline noise\n\t\treturn 0.001, 0.0\n\t}\n\n\tvar totalAmplitude float64\n\tvar totalPhase float64\n\tvar weight float64\n\n\tfor _, walker := range walkers {\n\t\t// Direct path contribution\n\t\tdirectAmp, directPhase := computeDirectPath(tx.Position, rx.Position, walker.Position, walls)\n\n\t\t// First-order reflection contribution (strongest reflected ray)\n\t\treflAmp, reflPhase := computeFirstOrderReflection(tx.Position, rx.Position, walker.Position, walls)\n\n\t\t// Combine direct and reflected paths (coherent sum for two-ray model)\n\t\t// The reflected ray interferes with the direct ray, creating constructive/destructive interference\n\t\tcombinedAmp := directAmp + reflAmp*math.Cos(directPhase-reflPhase)\n\t\tcombinedPhase := math.Atan2(\n\t\t\tdirectAmp*math.Sin(directPhase)+reflAmp*math.Sin(reflPhase),\n\t\t\tdirectAmp*math.Cos(directPhase)+reflAmp*math.Cos(reflPhase),\n\t\t)\n\n\t\t// Scale to reasonable values\n\t\tcombinedAmp *= 1000.0\n\n\t\t// Accumulate\n\t\ttotalAmplitude += combinedAmp\n\t\ttotalPhase += combinedPhase\n\t\tweight += 1.0\n\t}\n\n\t// Normalize phase\n\tif weight > 0 {\n\t\ttotalPhase /= weight\n\t}\n\n\treturn totalAmplitude, totalPhase\n}\n\n// computeDirectPath computes the CSI contribution from the direct path\n// through the walker to the receiver, using the log-distance path loss model.\nfunc computeDirectPath(tx, rx, walker Point, walls []Wall) (float64, float64) {\n\t// Distance from TX to walker\n\td1 := distance(tx, walker)\n\t// Distance from walker to RX\n\td2 := distance(walker, rx)\n\t// Total path length\n\tdTotal := d1 + d2\n\n\t// Direct TX-RX distance (for Fresnel zone calculation)\n\tdDirect := distance(tx, rx)\n\n\t// Path length excess for Fresnel zone calculation\n\texcess := dTotal - dDirect\n\tif excess < 0 {\n\t\texcess = 0\n\t}\n\n\t// Fresnel zone number\n\tzoneNumber := int(math.Ceil(excess / halfWavelength))\n\tif zoneNumber < 1 {\n\t\tzoneNumber = 1\n\t}\n\n\t// Zone decay (inverse square)\n\tdecay := 1.0 / math.Pow(float64(zoneNumber), 2.0)\n\n\t// Log-distance path loss model: PL(d) = PL_0 + 10*n*log10(d/d_0)\n\tvar pathLossDB float64\n\tif dTotal >= d0 {\n\t\tpathLossDB = pl0 + 10.0*n*math.Log10(dTotal/d0)\n\t} else {\n\t\t// For distances < d0, use free space approximation\n\t\tpathLossDB = pl0\n\t}\n\n\t// Wall attenuation on the direct path\n\twallLoss := computeWallLoss(tx, walker, walls)\n\twallLoss += computeWallLoss(walker, rx, walls)\n\n\t// Total loss in dB\n\ttotalLossDB := pathLossDB + wallLoss\n\n\t// Convert to linear amplitude\n\tamplitude := math.Pow(10.0, -totalLossDB/20.0)\n\n\t// Apply Fresnel zone decay\n\tamplitude *= decay\n\n\t// Phase at this position (based on total path length)\n\tphase := 2 * math.Pi * dTotal / wavelength\n\n\treturn amplitude, phase\n}\n\n// computeFirstOrderReflection computes the CSI contribution from the strongest\n// first-order reflection off a wall segment. Uses image method to find reflection point.\nfunc computeFirstOrderReflection(tx, rx, walker Point, walls []Wall) (float64, float64) {\n\tvar bestReflAmp float64\n\tvar bestReflPhase float64\n\tvar foundReflection bool\n\n\tfor _, wall := range walls {\n\t\t// Compute reflection point using image method\n\t\treflPoint, ok := findReflectionPoint(tx, rx, wall)\n\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Reflected path: TX -> reflection point -> RX\n\t\tdTxRefl := distance(tx, reflPoint)\n\t\tdReflRx := distance(reflPoint, rx)\n\t\tdReflTotal := dTxRefl + dReflRx\n\n\t\t// Direct path length (for comparison)\n\t\tdDirect := distance(tx, rx)\n\n\t\t// Log-distance path loss for reflected path\n\t\tvar pathLossDB float64\n\t\tif dReflTotal >= d0 {\n\t\t\tpathLossDB = pl0 + 10.0*n*math.Log10(dReflTotal/d0)\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tpathLossDB = pl0\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Wall attenuation (transmission loss through wall if any)\n\t\t// Plus reflection loss (weakest material first = lowest attenuation)\n\t\twallLoss := wall.Attenuation\n\n\t\t// Total loss in dB\n\t\ttotalLossDB := pathLossDB + wallLoss\n\n\t\t// Convert to linear amplitude\n\t\tamplitude := math.Pow(10.0, -totalLossDB/20.0)\n\n\t\t// Apply reflection coefficient (power coefficient)\n\t\tamplitude *= math.Sqrt(reflectionCoeff)\n\n\t\t// Normalize by direct path loss (so reflected ray is relative to direct)\n\t\tdirectPathLoss := pl0 + 10.0*n*math.Log10(dDirect/d0)\n\t\tamplitude *= math.Pow(10.0, (directPathLoss-pathLossDB)/20.0)\n\n\t\t// Phase based on reflected path length\n\t\tphase := 2 * math.Pi * dReflTotal / wavelength\n\n\t\t// Keep the strongest reflection (lowest attenuation)\n\t\tif !foundReflection || amplitude > bestReflAmp {\n\t\t\tbestReflAmp = amplitude\n\t\t\tbestReflPhase = phase\n\t\t\tfoundReflection = true\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif !foundReflection {\n\t\treturn 0, 0\n\t}\n\n\treturn bestReflAmp, bestReflPhase\n}\n\n// findReflectionPoint finds the specular reflection point on a wall segment\n// for a ray from TX to RX using the image method.\n// Returns the reflection point and true if a valid reflection exists, false otherwise.\nfunc findReflectionPoint(tx, rx Point, wall Wall) (Point, bool) {\n\t// For a vertical wall segment (in 2D floor plane), the reflection point\n\t// is found by reflecting the TX across the wall line and finding the\n\t// intersection with the wall segment.\n\n\t// Wall line equation: ax + by + c = 0\n\t// For vertical wall from (x1, y1) to (x2, y2):\n\t// If x1 == x2 (vertical wall), reflection is straightforward\n\tif math.Abs(wall.X1-wall.X2) < 1e-6 {\n\t\t// Vertical wall at x = wall.X1\n\t\t// Reflect TX across the wall\n\t\treflTxX := 2*wall.X1 - tx.X\n\t\treflTxY := tx.Y\n\n\t\t// Find intersection of line from reflTx to RX with the wall\n\t\t// Parametric line: reflTx + t*(rx - reflTx)\n\t\tdx := rx.X - reflTxX\n\t\tdy := rx.Y - reflTxY\n\n\t\tif math.Abs(dx) < 1e-6 {\n\t\t\t// Line is vertical, no intersection with vertical wall (or parallel)\n\t\t\treturn Point{}, false\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tt := (wall.X1 - reflTxX) / dx\n\n\t\t// Compute intersection point\n\t\tintersectY := reflTxY + t*dy\n\n\t\t// Check if intersection is within wall segment bounds\n\t\tminY := math.Min(wall.Y1, wall.Y2)\n\t\tmaxY := math.Max(wall.Y1, wall.Y2)\n\n\t\tif intersectY < minY || intersectY > maxY {\n\t\t\treturn Point{}, false\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Z coordinate is average of TX and RX Z (reflection in vertical plane)\n\t\tintersectZ := (tx.Z + rx.Z) / 2.0\n\n\t\treturn Point{X: wall.X1, Y: intersectY, Z: intersectZ}, true\n\t}\n\n\t// For horizontal wall segment (y1 == y2)\n\tif math.Abs(wall.Y1-wall.Y2) < 1e-6 {\n\t\t// Horizontal wall at y = wall.Y1\n\t\t// Reflect TX across the wall\n\t\treflTxX := tx.X\n\t\treflTxY := 2*wall.Y1 - tx.Y\n\n\t\t// Find intersection of line from reflTx to RX with the wall\n\t\tdx := rx.X - reflTxX\n\t\tdy := rx.Y - reflTxY\n\n\t\tif math.Abs(dy) < 1e-6 {\n\t\t\t// Line is horizontal, no intersection\n\t\t\treturn Point{}, false\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tt := (wall.Y1 - reflTxY) / dy\n\n\t\t// Compute intersection point\n\t\tintersectX := reflTxX + t*dx\n\n\t\t// Check if intersection is within wall segment bounds\n\t\tminX := math.Min(wall.X1, wall.X2)\n\t\tmaxX := math.Max(wall.X1, wall.X2)\n\n\t\tif intersectX < minX || intersectX > maxX {\n\t\t\treturn Point{}, false\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Z coordinate is average of TX and RX Z\n\t\tintersectZ := (tx.Z + rx.Z) / 2.0\n\n\t\treturn Point{X: intersectX, Y: wall.Y1, Z: intersectZ}, true\n\t}\n\n\t// General case: angled wall segment\n\t// Compute line intersection\n\t// Wall line: (x1, y1) to (x2, y2)\n\t// Ray from reflected TX to RX\n\n\t// Reflect TX across the wall line\n\treflTx := reflectPointAcrossLine(tx, Point{X: wall.X1, Y: wall.Y1, Z: 0}, Point{X: wall.X2, Y: wall.Y2, Z: 0})\n\n\t// Find intersection of line from reflTx to RX with the wall line\n\tintersect, ok := lineIntersection(\n\t\treflTx, rx,\n\t\tPoint{X: wall.X1, Y: wall.Y1, Z: 0}, Point{X: wall.X2, Y: wall.Y2, Z: 0},\n\t)\n\tif !ok {\n\t\treturn Point{}, false\n\t}\n\n\t// Check if intersection is within wall segment bounds\n\tminX := math.Min(wall.X1, wall.X2)\n\tmaxX := math.Max(wall.X1, wall.X2)\n\tminY := math.Min(wall.Y1, wall.Y2)\n\tmaxY := math.Max(wall.Y1, wall.Y2)\n\n\tif intersect.X < minX || intersect.X > maxX || intersect.Y < minY || intersect.Y > maxY {\n\t\treturn Point{}, false\n\t}\n\n\t// Z coordinate is average of TX and RX Z\n\tintersect.Z = (tx.Z + rx.Z) / 2.0\n\n\treturn intersect, true\n}\n\n// reflectPointAcrossLine reflects a point across a line defined by two points.\n// Uses the formula for reflection of a point across a line in 2D.\nfunc reflectPointAcrossLine(p, lineStart, lineEnd Point) Point {\n\t// Line direction vector\n\tlx := lineEnd.X - lineStart.X\n\tly := lineEnd.Y - lineStart.Y\n\n\t// Vector from line start to point\n\tpx := p.X - lineStart.X\n\tpy := p.Y - lineStart.Y\n\n\t// Project p onto the line (dot product)\n\tdot := px*lx + py*ly\n\tlenSq := lx*lx + ly*ly\n\n\tif lenSq < 1e-10 {\n\t\t// Line segment is too short\n\t\treturn p\n\t}\n\n\t// Projection parameter\n\tt := dot / lenSq\n\n\t// Closest point on line\n\tclosestX := lineStart.X + t*lx\n\tclosestY := lineStart.Y + t*ly\n\n\t// Reflected point: p' = closest + (closest - p) = 2*closest - p\n\treturn Point{\n\t\tX: 2*closestX - p.X,\n\t\tY: 2*closestY - p.Y,\n\t\tZ: p.Z,\n\t}\n}\n\n// lineIntersection finds the intersection point of two line segments in 2D.\n// Returns the intersection point and true if the lines intersect, false otherwise.\nfunc lineIntersection(p1, p2, p3, p4 Point) (Point, bool) {\n\t// Line 1: p1 to p2\n\t// Line 2: p3 to p4\n\n\tx1, y1 := p1.X, p1.Y\n\tx2, y2 := p2.X, p2.Y\n\tx3, y3 := p3.X, p3.Y\n\tx4, y4 := p4.X, p4.Y\n\n\t// Compute denominator\n\tdenom := (x1-x2)*(y3-y4) - (y1-y2)*(x3-x4)\n\tif math.Abs(denom) < 1e-10 {\n\t\t// Lines are parallel\n\t\treturn Point{}, false\n\t}\n\n\t// Compute intersection point using parametric form\n\tt := ((x1-x3)*(y3-y4) - (y1-y3)*(x3-x4)) / denom\n\tu := -((x1-x2)*(y1-y3) - (y1-y2)*(x1-x3)) / denom\n\n\t// Check if intersection is within both line segments\n\tif t < 0 || t > 1 || u < 0 || u > 1 {\n\t\treturn Point{}, false\n\t}\n\n\t// Compute intersection point\n\tintersectX := x1 + t*(x2-x1)\n\tintersectY := y1 + t*(y2-y1)\n\n\treturn Point{X: intersectX, Y: intersectY}, true\n}\n\n// distance computes Euclidean distance between two points\nfunc distance(a, b Point) float64 {\n\tdx := a.X - b.X\n\tdy := a.Y - b.Y\n\tdz := a.Z - b.Z\n\treturn math.Sqrt(dx*dx + dy*dy + dz*dz)\n}\n\n// computeWallLoss computes wall attenuation for a path through all walls.\n// For each wall the path intersects, add the wall's attenuation value.\nfunc computeWallLoss(from, to Point, walls []Wall) float64 {\n\ttotalLoss := 0.0\n\n\tfor _, wall := range walls {\n\t\tif pathIntersectsWall(from.X, from.Y, to.X, to.Y, wall.X1, wall.Y1, wall.X2, wall.Y2) {\n\t\t\ttotalLoss += wall.Attenuation\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn totalLoss\n}\n\n// pathIntersectsWall checks if a path intersects a wall segment (2D)\nfunc pathIntersectsWall(x1, y1, x2, y2, wx1, wy1, wx2, wy2 float64) bool {\n\t// Compute orientations\n\tccw := func(ax, ay, bx, by, cx, cy float64) float64 {\n\t\treturn (bx-ax)*(cy-ay) - (by-ay)*(cx-ax)\n\t}\n\n\to1 := ccw(x1, y1, x2, y2, wx1, wy1)\n\to2 := ccw(x1, y1, x2, y2, wx2, wy2)\n\to3 := ccw(wx1, wy1, wx2, wy2, x1, y1)\n\to4 := ccw(wx1, wy1, wx2, wy2, x2, y2)\n\n\t// Check for intersection\n\treturn o1*o2 < 0 && o3*o4 < 0\n}\n\n// amplitudeToRSSI converts amplitude to RSSI in dBm\nfunc amplitudeToRSSI(amplitude float64) int8 {\n\t// Convert amplitude to dBm (reference: amplitude 1.0 = -30 dBm)\n\tamplitudeDBm := -30.0 + 20.0*math.Log10(amplitude)\n\n\t// Clamp to realistic range\n\tif amplitudeDBm < -90 {\n\t\tamplitudeDBm = -90\n\t}\n\tif amplitudeDBm > -30 {\n\t\tamplitudeDBm = -30\n\t}\n\n\treturn int8(amplitudeDBm)\n}\n\n// generateIQPair generates a synthetic I/Q pair with Gaussian noise\nfunc generateIQPair(amplitude, phase float64, rng *rand.Rand) (int8, int8) {\n\t// Box-Muller transform for Gaussian noise\n\tu1 := rng.Float64()\n\tu2 := rng.Float64()\n\tz0 := math.Sqrt(-2.0*math.Log(u1)) * math.Cos(2.0*math.Pi*u2)\n\tz1 := math.Sqrt(-2.0*math.Log(u1)) * math.Sin(2.0*math.Pi*u2)\n\n\tnoiseI := z0 * *flagNoiseSigma\n\tnoiseQ := z1 * *flagNoiseSigma\n\n\t// Convert to I/Q\n\ti := amplitude*math.Cos(phase) + noiseI\n\tq := amplitude*math.Sin(phase) + noiseQ\n\n\t// Scale to int8 range\n\tscale := 127.0 / 10.0 // Scale factor\n\ti *= scale\n\tq *= scale\n\n\t// Clamp to int8 range [-127, 127]\n\tif i > 127 {\n\t\ti = 127\n\t}\n\tif i < -127 {\n\t\ti = -127\n\t}\n\tif q > 127 {\n\t\tq = 127\n\t}\n\tif q < -127 {\n\t\tq = -127\n\t}\n\n\treturn int8(i), int8(q)\n}\n","numLines":532,"startLine":1,"totalLines":532}}}

channel (1-14 for 2.4 GHz)\")\n60\t\tflagWalkerType  = flag.String(\"walker-type\", \"random\", \"Walker type: random, path, node-to-node\")\n61\t\tflagPathFile    = flag.String(\"path-file\", \"\", \"JSON file containing walker paths\")\n62\t\n63\t\t// Scenario flags\n64\t\tflagScenario     = flag.String(\"scenario\", \"normal\", \"Scenario type: normal, fall, ota, bag-on-couch\")\n65\t\tflagFallDelay    = flag.Duration(\"fall-delay\", 5*time.Second, \"Delay before fall triggers (fall scenario)\")\n66\t\tflagFallDuration = flag.Duration(\"fall-duration\", 800*time.Millisecond, \"Fall duration (fall scenario)\")\n67\t\tflagStillness    = flag.Duration(\"stillness\", 15*time.Second, \"Stillness duration after fall (fall scenario)\")\n68\t\tflagOTAVersion   = flag.String(\"ota-version\", \"sim-1.1.0\", \"Target firmware version (OTA scenario)\")\n69\t\tflagOTASize      = flag.Int64(\"ota-size\", 1024*1024, \"Firmware size in bytes (OTA scenario)\")\n70\t\tflagOTAFailure   = flag.Bool(\"ota-failure\", false, \"Simulate OTA boot failure for rollback (OTA scenario)\")\n71\t)\n72\t\n73\t// walls is populated from repeated --wall flags\n74\tvar walls []Wall\n75\t\n76\t// addWall is a custom flag value for repeated --wall flags\n77\ttype wallFlag struct{}\n78\t\n79\tfunc (w *wallFlag) String() string { return \"\" }\n80\tfunc (w *wallFlag) Set(value string) error {\n81\t\t// Format: x1,y1,x2,y2[:material]\n82\t\tparts := strings.Split(value, \",\")\n83\t\tif len(parts) < 4 {\n84\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"expected x1,y1,x2,y2[:material] format, got: %s\", value)\n85\t\t}\n86\t\tx1, err := strconv.ParseFloat(parts[0], 64)\n87\t\tif err != nil {\n88\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"invalid x1: %w\", err)\n89\t\t}\n90\t\ty1, err := strconv.ParseFloat(parts[1], 64)\n91\t\tif err != nil {\n92\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"invalid y1: %w\", err)\n93\t\t}\n94\t\tx2, err := strconv.ParseFloat(parts[2], 64)\n95\t\tif err != nil {\n96\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"invalid x2: %w\", err)\n97\t\t}\n98\t\ty2, err := strconv.ParseFloat(parts[3], 64)\n99\t\tif err != nil {\n100\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"invalid y2: %w\", err)\n101\t\t}\n102\t\n103\t\t// Parse material (default: drywall)\n104\t\tmaterial := MaterialDrywall\n105\t\tattenuation := 3.0\n106\t\tif len(parts) >= 5 {\n107\t\t\tmaterial = WallMaterial(strings.ToLower(parts[4]))\n108\t\t\tswitch material {\n109\t\t\tcase MaterialDrywall:\n110\t\t\t\tattenuation = 3.0\n111\t\t\tcase MaterialBrick, MaterialConcrete:\n112\t\t\t\tattenuation = 10.0\n113\t\t\tcase MaterialGlass:\n114\t\t\t\tattenuation = 2.0\n115\t\t\tcase MaterialMetal:\n116\t\t\t\tattenuation = 20.0\n117\t\t\tdefault:\n118\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"unknown material: %s (use: drywall, brick, concrete, glass, metal)\", parts[4])\n119\t\t\t}\n120\t\t}\n121\t\n122\t\twalls = append(walls, Wall{X1: x1, Y1: y1, X2: x2, Y2: y2, Material: material, Attenuation: attenuation})\n123\t\treturn nil\n124\t}\n125\t\n126\t// VirtualNode represents a simulated ESP32 node\n127\ttype VirtualNode struct {\n128\t\tID       int\n129\t\tMAC      [6]byte\n130\t\tPosition Point\n131\t\tRole     string // \"tx\", \"rx\", or \"tx_rx\"\n132\t\tConn     *websocket.Conn\n133\t\tmu       sync.Mutex\n134\t}\n135\t\n136\t// WalkerType defines how a walker moves\n137\ttype WalkerType string\n138\t\n139\tconst (\n140\t\tWalkerTypeRandomWalk  WalkerType = \"random\"\n141\t\tWalkerTypePathFollow  WalkerType = \"path\"\n142\t\tWalkerTypeNodeToNode  WalkerType = \"node-to-node\"\n143\t)\n144\t\n145\t// Walker represents a simulated person\n146\ttype Walker struct {\n147\t\tID       int\n148\t\tPosition Point\n149\t\tVelocity Point\n150\t\tSpeed    float64\n151\t\tHeight   float64\n152\t\tType     WalkerType\n153\t\tPath     []Point    // For path-following mode\n154\t\tPathIdx  int        // Current position along path\n155\t\tNodes    []*VirtualNode // For node-to-node mode\n156\t\tNodeIdx  int        // Current target node index\n157\t}\n158\t\n159\t// Point represents a 3D position\n160\ttype Point struct {\n161\t\tX, Y, Z float64\n162\t}\n163\t\n164\t// Space represents the room dimensions\n165\ttype Space struct {\n166\t\tWidth, Depth, Height float64\n167\t}\n168\t\n169\t// WallMaterial defines the type of wall material\n170\ttype WallMaterial string\n171\t\n172\tconst (\n173\t\tMaterialDrywall  WallMaterial = \"drywall\"\n174\t\tMaterialBrick    WallMaterial = \"brick\"\n175\t\tMaterialConcrete WallMaterial = \"concrete\"\n176\t\tMaterialGlass    WallMaterial = \"glass\"\n177\t\tMaterialMetal    WallMaterial = \"metal\"\n178\t)\n179\t\n180\t// Wall represents a wall segment with material properties\n181\ttype Wall struct {\n182\t\tX1, Y1, X2, Y2 float64\n183\t\tMaterial        WallMaterial\n184\t\tAttenuation     float64 // dB loss\n185\t}\n186\t\n187\t// Stats tracks simulation statistics\n188\ttype Stats struct {\n189\t\tFramesSent     atomic.Int64\n190\t\tFramesPerSec   float64\n191\t\tStartTime      time.Time\n192\t\tLastStatsTime  time.Time\n193\t\tLastFramesSent int64\n194\t}\n195\t\n196\tfunc main() {\n197\t\tflag.Var(&wallFlag{}, \"wall\", \"Add a wall as x1,y1,x2,y2 (can be repeated)\")\n198\t\tflag.Parse()\n199\t\n200\t\tlog.SetFlags(log.Ldate | log.Ltime | log.Lmicroseconds)\n201\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM] CSI Simulator CLI starting\")\n202\t\n203\t\t// Parse space dimensions\n204\t\tspace, err := parseSpace(*flagSpace)\n205\t\tif err != nil {\n206\t\t\tlog.Fatalf(\"[SIM] Invalid space dimensions: %v\", err)\n207\t\t}\n208\t\n209\t\t// Initialize random seed\n210\t\tif *flagSeed == 0 {\n211\t\t\t*flagSeed = time.Now().UnixNano()\n212\t\t}\n213\t\trng := rand.New(rand.NewSource(*flagSeed))\n214\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM] Random seed: %d\", *flagSeed)\n215\t\n216\t\t// Validate channel\n217\t\tif *flagChannel < 1 || *flagChannel > 14 {\n218\t\t\tlog.Fatalf(\"[SIM] Invalid channel: %d (must be 1-14)\", *flagChannel)\n219\t\t}\n220\t\n221\t\t// Create virtual nodes\n222\t\tnodes := createVirtualNodes(*flagNodes, space, rng)\n223\t\n224\t\t// Create walkers (may be nil for node-to-node mode)\n225\t\twalkers := createWalkers(*flagWalkers, space, rng)\n226\t\n227\t\t// For node-to-node mode, create walkers after nodes exist\n228\t\tif WalkerType(*flagWalkerType) == WalkerTypeNodeToNode {\n229\t\t\twalkers = createNodeToNodeWalkers(*flagWalkers, nodes)\n230\t\t}\n231\t\n232\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM] Configuration:\")\n233\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM]   Mothership: %s\", *flagMothership)\n234\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM]   Scenario: %s\", *flagScenario)\n235\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM]   Nodes: %d\", *flagNodes)\n236\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM]   Walkers: %d\", *flagWalkers)\n237\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM]   Rate: %d Hz\", *flagRate)\n238\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM]   Duration: %d s\", *flagDuration)\n239\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM]   Space: %.1fx%.1fx%.1f m\", space.Width, space.Depth, space.Height)\n240\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM]   Walls: %d\", len(walls))\n241\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM]   BLE: %v\", *flagBLE)\n242\t\n243\t\t// Create scenario configuration\n244\t\tscenarioConfig := &ScenarioConfig{\n245\t\t\tType:      ScenarioType(*flagScenario),\n246\t\t\tStartedAt: time.Now(),\n247\t\t\tFallParams: FallScenarioParams{\n248\t\t\t\tTriggerAfter:      *flagFallDelay,\n249\t\t\t\tDescentDuration:   *flagFallDuration,\n250\t\t\t\tStillnessDuration: *flagStillness,\n251\t\t\t\tMinVelocity:       -1.5, // Below -1.5 m/s threshold\n252\t\t\t\tMinZDrop:          0.8,  // At least 0.8m drop\n253\t\t\t\tEndZ:              0.3,  // Floor level\n254\t\t\t},\n255\t\t\tOTAParams: OTAScenarioParams{\n256\t\t\t\tUpdateAfter:      10 * time.Second,\n257\t\t\t\tFirmwareSize:     *flagOTASize,\n258\t\t\t\tNewVersion:       *flagOTAVersion,\n259\t\t\t\tRebootDelay:      3 * time.Second,\n260\t\t\t\tBootFailDuration: 30 * time.Second,\n261\t\t\t\tSimulateFailure:  *flagOTAFailure,\n262\t\t\t},\n263\t\t}\n264\t\n265\t\t// Create context for shutdown\n266\t\tctx, cancel := context.WithCancel(context.Background())\n267\t\tdefer cancel()\n268\t\n269\t\t// Handle interrupt signal\n270\t\tsigChan := make(chan os.Signal, 1)\n271\t\tsignal.Notify(sigChan, os.Interrupt)\n272\t\n273\t\t// Open CSV writer if specified\n274\t\tvar csvWriter *CSVWriter\n275\t\tif *flagOutputCSV != \"\" {\n276\t\t\tcsvWriter, err = NewCSVWriter(*flagOutputCSV)\n277\t\t\tif err != nil {\n278\t\t\t\tlog.Fatalf(\"[SIM] Failed to open CSV file: %v\", err)\n279\t\t\t}\n280\t\t\tdefer func() { _ = csvWriter.Close() }() //nolint:errcheck\n281\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM] Writing ground truth to %s\", *flagOutputCSV)\n282\t\t}\n283\t\n284\t\t// Start statistics reporter\n285\t\tstats := &Stats{StartTime: time.Now()}\n286\t\tgo reportStats(ctx, stats)\n287\t\n288\t\t// Connect all nodes to mothership\n289\t\tif err := connectNodes(ctx, nodes); err != nil {\n290\t\t\tlog.Fatalf(\"[SIM] Failed to connect nodes: %v\", err)\n291\t\t}\n292\t\tdefer closeAllNodes(nodes)\n293\t\n294\t\t// Main simulation loop\n295\t\tsimulationComplete := make(chan struct{})\n296\t\tgo runSimulation(ctx, nodes, walkers, space, rng, csvWriter, stats, simulationComplete, scenarioConfig)\n297\t\n298\t\t// Wait for completion or interrupt\n299\t\tvar durationTimer <-chan time.Time\n300\t\tif *flagDuration > 0 {\n301\t\t\tdurationTimer = time.After(time.Duration(*flagDuration) * time.Second)\n302\t\t} else {\n303\t\t\t// Never timeout if duration is 0\n304\t\t\tdurationTimer = make(chan time.Time)\n305\t\t}\n306\t\n307\t\tselect {\n308\t\tcase <-simulationComplete:\n309\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM] Simulation completed\")\n310\t\tcase <-sigChan:\n311\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM] Interrupted by user\")\n312\t\t\tcancel()\n313\t\tcase <-durationTimer:\n314\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM] Duration elapsed\")\n315\t\t\tcancel()\n316\t\t}\n317\t\n318\t\t// Verify blob count if requested\n319\t\tif *flagVerify {\n320\t\t\tif err := verifyBlobs(*flagWalkers, walkers, space); err != nil {\n321\t\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM] Verification FAILED: %v\", err)\n322\t\t\t\tos.Exit(1)\n323\t\t\t}\n324\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM] Verification PASSED\")\n325\t\t}\n326\t\n327\t\t// Print final statistics\n328\t\tprintFinalStats(stats, len(walkers))\n329\t}\n330\t\n331\t// parseSpace parses space dimensions from WxDxH format\n332\tfunc parseSpace(s string) (*Space, error) {\n333\t\tparts := strings.Split(s, \"x\")\n334\t\tif len(parts) != 3 {\n335\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"expected WxDxH format, got: %s\", s)\n336\t\t}\n337\t\twidth, err := strconv.ParseFloat(parts[0], 64)\n338\t\tif err != nil {\n339\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"invalid width: %w\", err)\n340\t\t}\n341\t\tdepth, err := strconv.ParseFloat(parts[1], 64)\n342\t\tif err != nil {\n343\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"invalid depth: %w\", err)\n344\t\t}\n345\t\theight, err := strconv.ParseFloat(parts[2], 64)\n346\t\tif err != nil {\n347\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"invalid height: %w\", err)\n348\t\t}\n349\t\treturn &Space{Width: width, Depth: depth, Height: height}, nil\n350\t}\n351\t\n352\t// createVirtualNodes creates virtual nodes positioned in the space\n353\tfunc createVirtualNodes(count int, space *Space, rng *rand.Rand) []*VirtualNode {\n354\t\tnodes := make([]*VirtualNode, count)\n355\t\n356\t\tfor i := 0; i < count; i++ {\n357\t\t\tnode := &VirtualNode{\n358\t\t\t\tID:   i,\n359\t\t\t\tMAC:  generateMAC(i),\n360\t\t\t\tRole: \"tx_rx\",\n361\t\t\t}\n362\t\n363\t\t\t// Distribute nodes around perimeter\n364\t\t\tperimeter := 2*(space.Width+space.Depth)\n365\t\t\tpos := float64(i) / float64(count) * perimeter\n366\t\n367\t\t\tif pos < space.Width {\n368\t\t\t\t// Bottom edge\n369\t\t\t\tnode.Position = Point{X: pos, Y: 0, Z: 2.0}\n370\t\t\t} else if pos < space.Width+space.Depth {\n371\t\t\t\t// Right edge\n372\t\t\t\tnode.Position = Point{X: space.Width, Y: pos - space.Width, Z: 2.0}\n373\t\t\t} else if pos < 2*space.Width+space.Depth {\n374\t\t\t\t// Top edge\n375\t\t\t\tnode.Position = Point{X: space.Width - (pos - space.Width - space.Depth), Y: space.Depth, Z: 2.0}\n376\t\t\t} else {\n377\t\t\t\t// Left edge\n378\t\t\t\tnode.Position = Point{X: 0, Y: space.Depth - (pos - 2*space.Width - space.Depth), Z: 2.0}\n379\t\t\t}\n380\t\n381\t\t\tnodes[i] = node\n382\t\t}\n383\t\n384\t\treturn nodes\n385\t}\n386\t\n387\t// generateMAC generates a synthetic MAC address for a virtual node\n388\tfunc generateMAC(id int) [6]byte {\n389\t\tvar mac [6]byte\n390\t\tmac[0] = 0xAA\n391\t\tmac[1] = 0xBB\n392\t\tmac[2] = 0xCC\n393\t\tmac[3] = byte((id >> 16) & 0xFF)\n394\t\tmac[4] = byte((id >> 8) & 0xFF)\n395\t\tmac[5] = byte(id & 0xFF)\n396\t\treturn mac\n397\t}\n398\t\n399\t// createWalkers creates synthetic walkers\n400\tfunc createWalkers(count int, space *Space, rng *rand.Rand) []*Walker {\n401\t\twalkerType := WalkerType(*flagWalkerType)\n402\t\n403\t\tif walkerType == WalkerTypePathFollow {\n404\t\t\treturn createPathWalkers(count, space)\n405\t\t}\n406\t\n407\t\tif walkerType == WalkerTypeNodeToNode {\n408\t\t\t// Will be created after nodes are initialized\n409\t\t\treturn nil\n410\t\t}\n411\t\n412\t\t// Default: random walk\n413\t\twalkers := make([]*Walker, count)\n414\t\n415\t\tfor i := 0; i < count; i++ {\n416\t\t\twalkers[i] = &Walker{\n417\t\t\t\tID:   i,\n418\t\t\t\tType: WalkerTypeRandomWalk,\n419\t\t\t\tPosition: Point{\n420\t\t\t\t\tX: rng.Float64() * space.Width,\n421\t\t\t\t\tY: rng.Float64() * space.Depth,\n422\t\t\t\t\tZ: 1.7,\n423\t\t\t\t},\n424\t\t\t\tVelocity: Point{\n425\t\t\t\t\tX: (rng.Float64() - 0.5) * 0.5,\n426\t\t\t\t\tY: (rng.Float64() - 0.5) * 0.5,\n427\t\t\t\t\tZ: 0,\n428\t\t\t\t},\n429\t\t\t\tSpeed:  0.8 + rng.Float64()*0.4,\n430\t\t\t\tHeight: 1.7,\n431\t\t\t}\n432\t\t}\n433\t\n434\t\treturn walkers\n435\t}\n436\t\n437\t// createPathWalkers creates walkers that follow predefined paths\n438\tfunc createPathWalkers(count int, space *Space) []*Walker {\n439\t\tif *flagPathFile == \"\" {\n440\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM] Path-following mode requires --path-file, using default rectangular path\")\n441\t\t\treturn createDefaultPathWalkers(count, space)\n442\t\t}\n443\t\n444\t\t// Load paths from JSON file\n445\t\tpaths, err := loadPathsFromFile(*flagPathFile)\n446\t\tif err != nil {\n447\t\t\tlog.Fatalf(\"[SIM] Failed to load paths from %s: %v\", *flagPathFile, err)\n448\t\t}\n449\t\n450\t\twalkers := make([]*Walker, count)\n451\t\tfor i := 0; i < count; i++ {\n452\t\t\t// Use path modulo count to allow fewer paths than walkers\n453\t\t\tpathIdx := i % len(paths)\n454\t\t\twalkers[i] = &Walker{\n455\t\t\t\tID:      i,\n456\t\t\t\tType:    WalkerTypePathFollow,\n457\t\t\t\tPath:    paths[pathIdx],\n458\t\t\t\tPathIdx: 0,\n459\t\t\t\tSpeed:   1.0,\n460\t\t\t\tHeight:  1.7,\n461\t\t\t}\n462\t\t\tif len(paths[pathIdx]) > 0 {\n463\t\t\t\twalkers[i].Position = paths[pathIdx][0]\n464\t\t\t}\n465\t\t}\n466\t\n467\t\treturn walkers\n468\t}\n469\t\n470\t// createDefaultPathWalkers creates walkers following a default rectangular perimeter path\n471\tfunc createDefaultPathWalkers(count int, space *Space) []*Walker {\n472\t\tmargin := 0.5\n473\t\tpath := []Point{\n474\t\t\t{X: margin, Y: margin, Z: 1.7},\n475\t\t\t{X: space.Width - margin, Y: margin, Z: 1.7},\n476\t\t\t{X: space.Width - margin, Y: space.Depth - margin, Z: 1.7},\n477\t\t\t{X: margin, Y: space.Depth - margin, Z: 1.7},\n478\t\t}\n479\t\n480\t\twalkers := make([]*Walker, count)\n481\t\tfor i := 0; i < count; i++ {\n482\t\t\tstartIdx := (i * len(path) / count) % len(path)\n483\t\t\twalkers[i] = &Walker{\n484\t\t\t\tID:      i,\n485\t\t\t\tType:    WalkerTypePathFollow,\n486\t\t\t\tPath:    path,\n487\t\t\t\tPathIdx: startIdx,\n488\t\t\t\tSpeed:   0.8 + 0.4*float64(i)/float64(count),\n489\t\t\t\tHeight:  1.7,\n490\t\t\t}\n491\t\t\tif len(path) > 0 {\n492\t\t\t\twalkers[i].Position = path[startIdx]\n493\t\t\t}\n494\t\t}\n495\t\n496\t\treturn walkers\n497\t}\n498\t\n499\t// createNodeToNodeWalkers creates walkers that traverse between virtual nodes\n500\tfunc createNodeToNodeWalkers(count int, nodes []*VirtualNode) []*Walker {\n501\t\tif len(nodes) < 2 {\n502\t\t\tlog.Fatalf(\"[SIM] Node-to-node mode requires at least 2 nodes\")\n503\t\t}\n504\t\n505\t\twalkers := make([]*Walker, count)\n506\t\tfor i := 0; i < count; i++ {\n507\t\t\twalkers[i] = &Walker{\n508\t\t\t\tID:      i,\n509\t\t\t\tType:    WalkerTypeNodeToNode,\n510\t\t\t\tNodes:   nodes,\n511\t\t\t\tNodeIdx: 1, // Target is second node\n512\t\t\t\tSpeed:   1.0,\n513\t\t\t\tHeight:  1.7,\n514\t\t\t}\n515\t\t\t// Start at first node\n516\t\t\tif len(nodes) > 0 {\n517\t\t\t\twalkers[i].Position = nodes[0].Position\n518\t\t\t}\n519\t\t}\n520\t\n521\t\treturn walkers\n522\t}\n523\t\n524\t// PathDefinition defines a walker path in JSON format\n525\ttype PathDefinition struct {\n526\t\tWaypoints []Point `json:\"waypoints\"` // Ordered list of points to visit\n527\t}\n528\t\n529\t// loadPathsFromFile loads walker paths from a JSON file\n530\tfunc loadPathsFromFile(filename string) ([][]Point, error) {\n531\t\tdata, err := os.ReadFile(filename)\n532\t\tif err != nil {\n533\t\t\treturn nil, err\n534\t\t}\n535\t\n536\t\tvar paths []PathDefinition\n537\t\tif err := json.Unmarshal(data, &paths); err != nil {\n538\t\t\treturn nil, err\n539\t\t}\n540\t\n541\t\tif len(paths) == 0 {\n542\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"no paths defined in file\")\n543\t\t}\n544\t\n545\t\tresult := make([][]Point, len(paths))\n546\t\tfor i, pathDef := range paths {\n547\t\t\tif len(pathDef.Waypoints) == 0 {\n548\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"path %d has no waypoints\", i)\n549\t\t\t}\n550\t\t\tresult[i] = pathDef.Waypoints\n551\t\t}\n552\t\n553\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM] Loaded %d paths from %s\", len(result), filename)\n554\t\treturn result, nil\n555\t}\n556\t\n557\t// connectNodes connects all virtual nodes to the mothership.\n558\t// Each node gets its own persistent connection with background goroutines\n559\t// for ping, health, and message reading.\n560\tfunc connectNodes(ctx context.Context, nodes []*VirtualNode) error {\n561\t\t// Get or generate token\n562\t\ttoken := *flagToken\n563\t\tif token == \"\" {\n564\t\t\tvar err error\n565\t\t\ttoken, err = provisionToken()\n566\t\t\tif err != nil {\n567\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to provision token: %w\", err)\n568\t\t\t}\n569\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM] Auto-provisioned token: %s...\", token[:min(16, len(token))])\n570\t\t}\n571\t\n572\t\t// Parse mothership URL\n573\t\twsURL, err := url.Parse(*flagMothership)\n574\t\tif err != nil {\n575\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"invalid mothership URL: %w\", err)\n576\t\t}\n577\t\n578\t\t// Convert http(s) to ws(s)\n579\t\tif wsURL.Scheme == \"http\" {\n580\t\t\twsURL.Scheme = \"ws\"\n581\t\t} else if wsURL.Scheme == \"https\" {\n582\t\t\twsURL.Scheme = \"wss\"\n583\t\t}\n584\t\n585\t\terrChan := make(chan error, len(nodes))\n586\t\n587\t\tfor _, node := range nodes {\n588\t\t\t// Add node WS path if needed\n589\t\t\tnodeURL := wsURL.String()\n590\t\t\tif !strings.Contains(nodeURL, \"/ws/\") && !strings.HasSuffix(nodeURL, \"/ws\") {\n591\t\t\t\tif strings.HasSuffix(nodeURL, \"/\") {\n592\t\t\t\t\tnodeURL = nodeURL + \"ws\"\n593\t\t\t\t} else {\n594\t\t\t\t\tnodeURL = nodeURL + \"/ws\"\n595\t\t\t\t}\n596\t\t\t}\n597\t\n598\t\t\theaders := http.Header{}\n599\t\t\theaders.Set(\"X-Spaxel-Token\", token)\n600\t\n601\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM] Node %d connecting to %s\", node.ID, nodeURL)\n602\t\n603\t\t\tconn, resp, err := websocket.DefaultDialer.DialContext(ctx, nodeURL, headers)\n604\t\t\tif err != nil {\n605\t\t\t\tif resp != nil {\n606\t\t\t\t\tbody, _ := io.ReadAll(resp.Body)\n607\t\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"node %d dial failed: %w (status %d: %s)\", node.ID, err, resp.StatusCode, string(body))\n608\t\t\t\t}\n609\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"node %d dial failed: %w\", node.ID, err)\n610\t\t\t}\n611\t\n612\t\t\tnode.Conn = conn\n613\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM] Node %d connected\", node.ID)\n614\t\n615\t\t\t// Send hello message\n616\t\t\thello := map[string]interface{}{\n617\t\t\t\t\"type\":             \"hello\",\n618\t\t\t\t\"mac\":              macToString(node.MAC),\n619\t\t\t\t\"firmware_version\": \"sim-1.0.0\",\n620\t\t\t\t\"capabilities\":     []string{\"csi\", \"tx\", \"rx\"},\n621\t\t\t\t\"chip\":             \"ESP32-S3\",\n622\t\t\t\t\"flash_mb\":         16,\n623\t\t\t\t\"uptime_ms\":        1000,\n624\t\t\t\t\"wifi_rssi\":        -45,\n625\t\t\t\t\"ip\":               fmt.Sprintf(\"127.0.0.%d\", node.ID+2),\n626\t\t\t}\n627\t\n628\t\t\thelloBytes, err := json.Marshal(hello)\n629\t\t\tif err != nil {\n630\t\t\t\tconn.Close() //nolint:errcheck\n631\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"node %d marshal hello: %w\", node.ID, err)\n632\t\t\t}\n633\t\n634\t\t\tnode.mu.Lock()\n635\t\t\terr = conn.WriteMessage(websocket.TextMessage, helloBytes)\n636\t\t\tnode.mu.Unlock()\n637\t\n638\t\t\tif err != nil {\n639\t\t\t\tconn.Close() //nolint:errcheck\n640\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"node %d send hello: %w\", node.ID, err)\n641\t\t\t}\n642\t\n643\t\t\t// Wait for role assignment\n644\t\t\tconn.SetReadDeadline(time.Now().Add(10 * time.Second)) //nolint:errcheck\n645\t\t\t_, message, err := conn.ReadMessage()\n646\t\t\tif err != nil {\n647\t\t\t\tconn.Close() //nolint:errcheck\n648\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"node %d read role: %w\", node.ID, err)\n649\t\t\t}\n650\t\n651\t\t\tvar roleMsg map[string]interface{}\n652\t\t\tif err := json.Unmarshal(message, &roleMsg); err != nil {\n653\t\t\t\tconn.Close() //nolint:errcheck\n654\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"node %d parse role: %w\", node.ID, err)\n655\t\t\t}\n656\t\n657\t\t\tif roleMsg[\"type\"] == \"reject\" {\n658\t\t\t\tconn.Close() //nolint:errcheck\n659\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"node %d rejected: %v\", node.ID, roleMsg[\"reason\"])\n660\t\t\t}\n661\t\n662\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM] Node %d received role: %v\", node.ID, roleMsg[\"role\"])\n663\t\n664\t\t\t// Start background goroutines for this connection\n665\t\t\tstartTime := time.Now()\n666\t\t\tgo node.pingLoop(ctx)\n667\t\t\tgo node.healthLoop(ctx, startTime)\n668\t\t\tgo node.readLoop(ctx, errChan)\n669\t\t}\n670\t\n671\t\treturn nil\n672\t}\n673\t\n674\t// provisionToken provisions a token. Tries the mothership API first,\n675\t// falls back to a synthetic HMAC token.\n676\tfunc provisionToken() (string, error) {\n677\t\t// Parse mothership URL to get HTTP endpoint\n678\t\twsURL, err := url.Parse(*flagMothership)\n679\t\tif err != nil {\n680\t\t\treturn \"\", fmt.Errorf(\"invalid mothership URL: %w\", err)\n681\t\t}\n682\t\n683\t\thttpURL := *wsURL\n684\t\tif httpURL.Scheme == \"ws\" {\n685\t\t\thttpURL.Scheme = \"http\"\n686\t\t} else if httpURL.Scheme == \"wss\" {\n687\t\t\thttpURL.Scheme = \"https\"\n688\t\t}\n689\t\n690\t\t// Trim /ws suffix to get base URL\n691\t\tbaseURL := strings.TrimSuffix(httpURL.String(), \"/ws\")\n692\t\tbaseURL = strings.TrimSuffix(baseURL, \"/\")\n693\t\tprovisionURL := baseURL + \"/api/provision\"\n694\t\n695\t\t// Try POST /api/provision with synthetic credentials\n696\t\tbody := strings.NewReader(`{\"mac\":\"AA:BB:CC:00:00:00\"}`)\n697\t\tresp, err := http.Post(provisionURL, \"application/json\", body)\n698\t\tif err == nil && resp.StatusCode == http.StatusOK {\n699\t\t\tvar result map[string]interface{}\n700\t\t\tif json.NewDecoder(resp.Body).Decode(&result) == nil {\n701\t\t\t\t_ = resp.Body.Close()\n702\t\t\t\tif token, ok := result[\"node_token\"].(string); ok && token != \"\" {\n703\t\t\t\t\treturn token, nil\n704\t\t\t\t}\n705\t\t\t}\n706\t\t}\n707\t\tif resp != nil {\n708\t\t\t_ = resp.Body.Close()\n709\t\t}\n710\t\n711\t\t// Fallback: generate synthetic token\n712\t\th := hmac.New(sha256.New, []byte(\"sim-install-secret\"))\n713\t\th.Write([]byte(\"sim-node\"))\n714\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%064x\", h.Sum(nil)), nil\n715\t}\n716\t\n717\t// closeAllNodes closes all node WebSocket connections\n718\tfunc closeAllNodes(nodes []*VirtualNode) {\n719\t\tfor _, node := range nodes {\n720\t\t\tif node.Conn != nil {\n721\t\t\t\tnode.mu.Lock()\n722\t\t\t\tnode.Conn.WriteMessage(websocket.CloseMessage, //nolint:errcheck\n723\t\t\t\t\twebsocket.FormatCloseMessage(websocket.CloseNormalClosure, \"sim shutdown\"))\n724\t\t\t\tnode.Conn.Close() //nolint:errcheck\n725\t\t\t\tnode.mu.Unlock()\n726\t\t\t}\n727\t\t}\n728\t}\n729\t\n730\t// macToString converts a 6-byte MAC to colon-separated hex\n731\tfunc macToString(mac [6]byte) string {\n732\t\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%02X:%02X:%02X:%02X:%02X:%02X\",\n733\t\t\tmac[0], mac[1], mac[2], mac[3], mac[4], mac[5])\n734\t}\n735\t\n736\t// pingLoop sends WebSocket pings\n737\tfunc (n *VirtualNode) pingLoop(ctx context.Context) {\n738\t\tticker := time.NewTicker(30 * time.Second)\n739\t\tdefer ticker.Stop()\n740\t\n741\t\tfor {\n742\t\t\tselect {\n743\t\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n744\t\t\t\treturn\n745\t\t\tcase <-ticker.C:\n746\t\t\t\tn.mu.Lock()\n747\t\t\t\terr := n.Conn.WriteMessage(websocket.PingMessage, nil)\n748\t\t\t\tn.mu.Unlock()\n749\t\n750\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n751\t\t\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM] Node %d ping failed: %v\", n.ID, err)\n752\t\t\t\t\treturn\n753\t\t\t\t}\n754\t\t\t}\n755\t\t}\n756\t}\n757\t\n758\t// healthLoop sends periodic health messages\n759\tfunc (n *VirtualNode) healthLoop(ctx context.Context, startTime time.Time) {\n760\t\tticker := time.NewTicker(10 * time.Second)\n761\t\tdefer ticker.Stop()\n762\t\n763\t\tfor {\n764\t\t\tselect {\n765\t\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n766\t\t\t\treturn\n767\t\t\tcase <-ticker.C:\n768\t\t\t\thealth := map[string]interface{}{\n769\t\t\t\t\t\"type\":            \"health\",\n770\t\t\t\t\t\"mac\":             macToString(n.MAC),\n771\t\t\t\t\t\"timestamp_ms\":    time.Now().UnixMilli(),\n772\t\t\t\t\t\"free_heap_bytes\": 200000,\n773\t\t\t\t\t\"wifi_rssi_dbm\":   -45,\n774\t\t\t\t\t\"uptime_ms\":       time.Since(startTime).Milliseconds(),\n775\t\t\t\t\t\"csi_rate_hz\":     *flagRate,\n776\t\t\t\t\t\"wifi_channel\":    *flagChannel,\n777\t\t\t\t}\n778\t\n779\t\t\t\thealthBytes, err := json.Marshal(health)\n780\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n781\t\t\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM] Node %d marshal health: %v\", n.ID, err)\n782\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n783\t\t\t\t}\n784\t\n785\t\t\t\tn.mu.Lock()\n786\t\t\t\terr = n.Conn.WriteMessage(websocket.TextMessage, healthBytes)\n787\t\t\t\tn.mu.Unlock()\n788\t\n789\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n790\t\t\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM] Node %d send health failed: %v\", n.ID, err)\n791\t\t\t\t\treturn\n792\t\t\t\t}\n793\t\t\t}\n794\t\t}\n795\t}\n796\t\n797\t// readLoop reads downstream messages from the WebSocket\n798\tfunc (n *VirtualNode) readLoop(ctx context.Context, errChan chan<- error) {\n799\t\tfor {\n800\t\t\tselect {\n801\t\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n802\t\t\t\treturn\n803\t\t\tdefault:\n804\t\t\t}\n805\t\n806\t\t\tn.mu.Lock()\n807\t\t\tconn := n.Conn\n808\t\t\tn.mu.Unlock()\n809\t\n810\t\t\tif conn == nil {\n811\t\t\t\treturn\n812\t\t\t}\n813\t\n814\t\t\tconn.SetReadDeadline(time.Now().Add(60 * time.Second)) //nolint:errcheck\n815\t\t\t_, message, err := conn.ReadMessage()\n816\t\t\tif err != nil {\n817\t\t\t\tselect {\n818\t\t\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n819\t\t\t\t\treturn\n820\t\t\t\tdefault:\n821\t\t\t\t}\n822\t\t\t\tif websocket.IsCloseError(err) {\n823\t\t\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM] Node %d connection closed\", n.ID)\n824\t\t\t\t\treturn\n825\t\t\t\t}\n826\t\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM] Node %d read error: %v\", n.ID, err)\n827\t\t\t\treturn\n828\t\t\t}\n829\t\n830\t\t\tvar msg map[string]interface{}\n831\t\t\tif err := json.Unmarshal(message, &msg); err != nil {\n832\t\t\t\tcontinue\n833\t\t\t}\n834\t\n835\t\t\tmsgType, ok := msg[\"type\"].(string)\n836\t\t\tif !ok {\n837\t\t\t\tcontinue\n838\t\t\t}\n839\t\n840\t\t\tswitch msgType {\n841\t\t\tcase \"role\":\n842\t\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM] Node %d role update: %v\", n.ID, msg[\"role\"])\n843\t\t\tcase \"config\":\n844\t\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM] Node %d config update: %v\", n.ID, msg)\n845\t\t\tcase \"reject\":\n846\t\t\t\terrChan <- fmt.Errorf(\"node %d rejected: %v\", n.ID, msg[\"reason\"])\n847\t\t\t\treturn\n848\t\t\tcase \"shutdown\":\n849\t\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM] Node %d received shutdown\", n.ID)\n850\t\t\t\treturn\n851\t\t\t}\n852\t\t}\n853\t}\n854\t\n855\t// runSimulation runs the main CSI generation loop\n856\tfunc runSimulation(ctx context.Context, nodes []*VirtualNode, walkers []*Walker, space *Space, rng *rand.Rand, csvWriter *CSVWriter, stats *Stats, done chan<- struct{}, scenario *ScenarioConfig) {\n857\t\tdefer close(done)\n858\t\n859\t\tticker := time.NewTicker(time.Duration(1000/(*flagRate)) * time.Millisecond)\n860\t\tdefer ticker.Stop()\n861\t\n862\t\tframeNum := 0\n863\t\tlastBLETime := time.Now()\n864\t\n865\t\t// Initialize fall scenario state\n866\t\tvar fallState *FallScenarioState\n867\t\tif scenario.Type == ScenarioFall || scenario.Type == ScenarioBagOnCouch {\n868\t\t\tif len(walkers) > 0 {\n869\t\t\t\tfallState = &FallScenarioState{\n870\t\t\t\t\tWalker: walkers[0],\n871\t\t\t\t\tState:  \"walking\",\n872\t\t\t\t}\n873\t\t\t\tif scenario.Type == ScenarioBagOnCouch {\n874\t\t\t\t\t// For bag-on-couch, start with a lower position\n875\t\t\t\t\twalkers[0].Position.Z = 1.0\n876\t\t\t\t\twalkers[0].Velocity.Z = -0.2 // Slow descent\n877\t\t\t\t}\n878\t\t\t}\n879\t\t}\n880\t\n881\t\t// Track scenario timing\n882\t\tscenarioStarted := false\n883\t\n884\t\tfor {\n885\t\t\tselect {\n886\t\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n887\t\t\t\treturn\n888\t\t\tcase <-ticker.C:\n889\t\t\t\t// Handle fall scenario timing\n890\t\t\t\tif fallState != nil && !scenarioStarted && time.Since(scenario.StartedAt) >= scenario.FallParams.TriggerAfter {\n891\t\t\t\t\tif scenario.Type == ScenarioFall {\n892\t\t\t\t\t\tfallState.StartFall(scenario.FallParams)\n893\t\t\t\t\t\tscenarioStarted = true\n894\t\t\t\t\t}\n895\t\t\t\t}\n896\t\n897\t\t\t\t// Update walker positions\n898\t\t\t\tif fallState != nil {\n899\t\t\t\t\tdt := 1.0 / float64(*flagRate)\n900\t\t\t\t\tfallState.UpdateForFallScenario(dt, scenario.FallParams, space, rng)\n901\t\t\t\t} else {\n902\t\t\t\t\tupdateWalkers(walkers, space, rng)\n903\t\t\t\t}\n904\t\n905\t\t\t\t// Write to CSV\n906\t\t\t\tif csvWriter != nil {\n907\t\t\t\t\tcsvWriter.WriteRow(walkers, nodes, walls)\n908\t\t\t\t}\n909\t\n910\t\t\t\t// Send CSI frames for each node pair\n911\t\t\t\tfor _, txNode := range nodes {\n912\t\t\t\t\tfor _, rxNode := range nodes {\n913\t\t\t\t\t\tif txNode.ID == rxNode.ID {\n914\t\t\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n915\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n916\t\n917\t\t\t\t\t\tframe := generateCSIFrame(txNode, rxNode, walkers, walls, frameNum, rng)\n918\t\n919\t\t\t\t\t\ttxNode.mu.Lock()\n920\t\t\t\t\t\terr := txNode.Conn.WriteMessage(websocket.BinaryMessage, frame)\n921\t\t\t\t\t\ttxNode.mu.Unlock()\n922\t\n923\t\t\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n924\t\t\t\t\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM] Node %d send CSI failed: %v\", txNode.ID, err)\n925\t\t\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n926\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n927\t\n928\t\t\t\t\t\tstats.FramesSent.Add(1)\n929\t\t\t\t\t}\n930\t\t\t\t}\n931\t\n932\t\t\t\t// Send BLE messages if enabled\n933\t\t\t\tif *flagBLE && time.Since(lastBLETime) > 5*time.Second {\n934\t\t\t\t\tsendBLEMessages(nodes, walkers)\n935\t\t\t\t\tlastBLETime = time.Now()\n936\t\t\t\t}\n937\t\n938\t\t\t\tframeNum++\n939\t\t\t}\n940\t\t}\n941\t}\n942\t\n943\t// updateWalkers updates walker positions based on their movement type\n944\tfunc updateWalkers(walkers []*Walker, space *Space, rng *rand.Rand) {\n945\t\tdt := 1.0 / float64(*flagRate)\n946\t\n947\t\tfor _, walker := range walkers {\n948\t\t\tswitch walker.Type {\n949\t\t\tcase WalkerTypePathFollow:\n950\t\t\t\tupdatePathWalker(walker, dt)\n951\t\t\tcase WalkerTypeNodeToNode:\n952\t\t\t\tupdateNodeToNodeWalker(walker, dt, space)\n953\t\t\tcase WalkerTypeRandomWalk:\n954\t\t\t\tupdateRandomWalker(walker, dt, space, rng)\n955\t\t\t}\n956\t\t}\n957\t}\n958\t\n959\t// updateRandomWalker implements random walk motion\n960\tfunc updateRandomWalker(walker *Walker, dt float64, space *Space, rng *rand.Rand) {\n961\t\twalker.Position.X += walker.Velocity.X * dt\n962\t\twalker.Position.Y += walker.Velocity.Y * dt\n963\t\n964\t\t// Bounce off walls\n965\t\tmargin := 0.2\n966\t\tif walker.Position.X < margin {\n967\t\t\twalker.Position.X = margin\n968\t\t\twalker.Velocity.X *= -1\n969\t\t}\n970\t\tif walker.Position.X > space.Width-margin {\n971\t\t\twalker.Position.X = space.Width - margin\n972\t\t\twalker.Velocity.X *= -1\n973\t\t}\n974\t\tif walker.Position.Y < margin {\n975\t\t\twalker.Position.Y = margin\n976\t\t\twalker.Velocity.Y *= -1\n977\t\t}\n978\t\tif walker.Position.Y > space.Depth-margin {\n979\t\t\twalker.Position.Y = space.Depth - margin\n980\t\t\twalker.Velocity.Y *= -1\n981\t\t}\n982\t\n983\t\t// Random velocity perturbation\n984\t\tperturbation := 0.1\n985\t\twalker.Velocity.X += (rng.Float64() - 0.5) * perturbation\n986\t\twalker.Velocity.Y += (rng.Float64() - 0.5) * perturbation\n987\t\n988\t\t// Clamp velocity\n989\t\tspeed := walker.Speed * (0.5 + rng.Float64()*0.5)\n990\t\tcurrentSpeed := math.Sqrt(walker.Velocity.X*walker.Velocity.X + walker.Velocity.Y*walker.Velocity.Y)\n991\t\tif currentSpeed > 0 {\n992\t\t\twalker.Velocity.X = (walker.Velocity.X / currentSpeed) * speed\n993\t\t\twalker.Velocity.Y = (walker.Velocity.Y / currentSpeed) * speed\n994\t\t}\n995\t\n996\t\twalker.Position.Z = walker.Height\n997\t}\n998\t\n999\t// updatePathWalker implements path-following motion\n1000\tfunc updatePathWalker(walker *Walker, dt float64) {\n1001\t\tif len(walker.Path) == 0 {\n1002\t\t\treturn\n1003\t\t}\n1004\t\n1005\t\ttarget := walker.Path[walker.PathIdx]\n1006\t\tdx := target.X - walker.Position.X\n1007\t\tdy := target.Y - walker.Position.Y\n1008\t\tdz := target.Z - walker.Position.Z\n1009\t\tdist := math.Sqrt(dx*dx + dy*dy + dz*dz)\n1010\t\n1011\t\t// If very close to target, move to next waypoint\n1012\t\tif dist < 0.1 {\n1013\t\t\twalker.PathIdx = (walker.PathIdx + 1) % len(walker.Path)\n1014\t\t\treturn\n1015\t\t}\n1016\t\n1017\t\t// Move towards target at constant speed\n1018\t\tmoveDist := walker.Speed * dt\n1019\t\tif moveDist > dist {\n1020\t\t\tmoveDist = dist\n1021\t\t}\n1022\t\n1023\t\tt := moveDist / dist\n1024\t\twalker.Position.X += dx * t\n1025\t\twalker.Position.Y += dy * t\n1026\t\n1027\t\t// Update velocity vector for consistency\n1028\t\tif dist > 0 {\n1029\t\t\twalker.Velocity.X = (dx / dist) * walker.Speed\n1030\t\t\twalker.Velocity.Y = (dy / dist) * walker.Speed\n1031\t\t\twalker.Velocity.Z = (dz / dist) * walker.Speed\n1032\t\t}\n1033\t}\n1034\t\n1035\t// updateNodeToNodeWalker implements traversal between virtual nodes\n1036\tfunc updateNodeToNodeWalker(walker *Walker, dt float64, space *Space) {\n1037\t\tif len(walker.Nodes) < 2 {\n1038\t\t\tupdateRandomWalker(walker, dt, space, rand.New(rand.NewSource(time.Now().UnixNano())))\n1039\t\t\treturn\n1040\t\t}\n1041\t\n1042\t\ttargetNode := walker.Nodes[walker.NodeIdx]\n1043\t\ttargetPos := targetNode.Position\n1044\t\n1045\t\tdx := targetPos.X - walker.Position.X\n1046\t\tdy := targetPos.Y - walker.Position.Y\n1047\t\tdz := targetPos.Z - walker.Position.Z\n1048\t\tdist := math.Sqrt(dx*dx + dy*dy + dz*dz)\n1049\t\n1050\t\t// Check if we've arrived at the target node (horizontal distance)\n1051\t\thorizontalDist := math.Sqrt(dx*dx + dy*dy)\n1052\t\tif horizontalDist < 0.3 {\n1053\t\t\t// Move to next node\n1054\t\t\twalker.NodeIdx = (walker.NodeIdx + 1) % len(walker.Nodes)\n1055\t\t\treturn\n1056\t\t}\n1057\t\n1058\t\t// Move towards target node\n1059\t\tmoveDist := walker.Speed * dt\n1060\t\tif moveDist > horizontalDist {\n1061\t\t\tmoveDist = horizontalDist\n1062\t\t}\n1063\t\n1064\t\tt := moveDist / horizontalDist\n1065\t\twalker.Position.X += dx * t\n1066\t\twalker.Position.Y += dy * Z: 1.7},\n\t\t{X: margin, Y: space.Depth - margin, Z: 1.7},\n\t}\n\n\twalkers := make([]*Walker, count)\n\tfor i := 0; i < count; i++ {\n\t\tstartIdx := (i * len(path) / count) % len(path)\n\t\twalkers[i] = &Walker{\n\t\t\tID:      i,\n\t\t\tType:    WalkerTypePathFollow,\n\t\t\tPath:    path,\n\t\t\tPathIdx: startIdx,\n\t\t\tSpeed:   0.8 + 0.4*float64(i)/float64(count),\n\t\t\tHeight:  1.7,\n\t\t}\n\t\tif len(path) > 0 {\n\t\t\twalkers[i].Position = path[startIdx]\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn walkers\n}\n\n// createNodeToNodeWalkers creates walkers that traverse between virtual nodes\nfunc createNodeToNodeWalkers(count int, nodes []*VirtualNode) []*Walker {\n\tif len(nodes) < 2 {\n\t\tlog.Fatalf(\"[SIM] Node-to-node mode requires at least 2 nodes\")\n\t}\n\n\twalkers := make([]*Walker, count)\n\tfor i := 0; i < count; i++ {\n\t\twalkers[i] = &Walker{\n\t\t\tID:      i,\n\t\t\tType:    WalkerTypeNodeToNode,\n\t\t\tNodes:   nodes,\n\t\t\tNodeIdx: 1, // Target is second node\n\t\t\tSpeed:   1.0,\n\t\t\tHeight:  1.7,\n\t\t}\n\t\t// Start at first node\n\t\tif len(nodes) > 0 {\n\t\t\twalkers[i].Position = nodes[0].Position\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn walkers\n}\n\n// PathDefinition defines a walker path in JSON format\ntype PathDefinition struct {\n\tWaypoints []Point `json:\"waypoints\"` // Ordered list of points to visit\n}\n\n// loadPathsFromFile loads walker paths from a JSON file\nfunc loadPathsFromFile(filename string) ([][]Point, error) {\n\tdata, err := os.ReadFile(filename)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tvar paths []PathDefinition\n\tif err := json.Unmarshal(data, &paths); err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tif len(paths) == 0 {\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"no paths defined in file\")\n\t}\n\n\tresult := make([][]Point, len(paths))\n\tfor i, pathDef := range paths {\n\t\tif len(pathDef.Waypoints) == 0 {\n\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"path %d has no waypoints\", i)\n\t\t}\n\t\tresult[i] = pathDef.Waypoints\n\t}\n\n\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM] Loaded %d paths from %s\", len(result), filename)\n\treturn result, nil\n}\n\n// connectNodes connects all virtual nodes to the mothership.\n// Each node gets its own persistent connection with background goroutines\n// for ping, health, and message reading.\nfunc connectNodes(ctx context.Context, nodes []*VirtualNode) error {\n\t// Get or generate token\n\ttoken := *flagToken\n\tif token == \"\" {\n\t\tvar err error\n\t\ttoken, err = provisionToken()\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to provision token: %w\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM] Auto-provisioned token: %s...\", token[:min(16, len(token))])\n\t}\n\n\t// Parse mothership URL\n\twsURL, err := url.Parse(*flagMothership)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"invalid mothership URL: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\n\t// Convert http(s) to ws(s)\n\tif wsURL.Scheme == \"http\" {\n\t\twsURL.Scheme = \"ws\"\n\t} else if wsURL.Scheme == \"https\" {\n\t\twsURL.Scheme = \"wss\"\n\t}\n\n\terrChan := make(chan error, len(nodes))\n\n\tfor _, node := range nodes {\n\t\t// Add node WS path if needed\n\t\tnodeURL := wsURL.String()\n\t\tif !strings.Contains(nodeURL, \"/ws/\") && !strings.HasSuffix(nodeURL, \"/ws\") {\n\t\t\tif strings.HasSuffix(nodeURL, \"/\") {\n\t\t\t\tnodeURL = nodeURL + \"ws\"\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\tnodeURL = nodeURL + \"/ws\"\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\theaders := http.Header{}\n\t\theaders.Set(\"X-Spaxel-Token\", token)\n\n\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM] Node %d connecting to %s\", node.ID, nodeURL)\n\n\t\tconn, resp, err := websocket.DefaultDialer.DialContext(ctx, nodeURL, headers)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tif resp != nil {\n\t\t\t\tbody, _ := io.ReadAll(resp.Body)\n\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"node %d dial failed: %w (status %d: %s)\", node.ID, err, resp.StatusCode, string(body))\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"node %d dial failed: %w\", node.ID, err)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tnode.Conn = conn\n\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM] Node %d connected\", node.ID)\n\n\t\t// Send hello message\n\t\thello := map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\"type\":             \"hello\",\n\t\t\t\"mac\":              macToString(node.MAC),\n\t\t\t\"firmware_version\": \"sim-1.0.0\",\n\t\t\t\"capabilities\":     []string{\"csi\", \"tx\", \"rx\"},\n\t\t\t\"chip\":             \"ESP32-S3\",\n\t\t\t\"flash_mb\":         16,\n\t\t\t\"uptime_ms\":        1000,\n\t\t\t\"wifi_rssi\":        -45,\n\t\t\t\"ip\":               fmt.Sprintf(\"127.0.0.%d\", node.ID+2),\n\t\t}\n\n\t\thelloBytes, err := json.Marshal(hello)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tconn.Close() //nolint:errcheck\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"node %d marshal hello: %w\", node.ID, err)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tnode.mu.Lock()\n\t\terr = conn.WriteMessage(websocket.TextMessage, helloBytes)\n\t\tnode.mu.Unlock()\n\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tconn.Close() //nolint:errcheck\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"node %d send hello: %w\", node.ID, err)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Wait for role assignment\n\t\tconn.SetReadDeadline(time.Now().Add(10 * time.Second)) //nolint:errcheck\n\t\t_, message, err := conn.ReadMessage()\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tconn.Close() //nolint:errcheck\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"node %d read role: %w\", node.ID, err)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tvar roleMsg map[string]interface{}\n\t\tif err := json.Unmarshal(message, &roleMsg); err != nil {\n\t\t\tconn.Close() //nolint:errcheck\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"node %d parse role: %w\", node.ID, err)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif roleMsg[\"type\"] == \"reject\" {\n\t\t\tconn.Close() //nolint:errcheck\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"node %d rejected: %v\", node.ID, roleMsg[\"reason\"])\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM] Node %d received role: %v\", node.ID, roleMsg[\"role\"])\n\n\t\t// Start background goroutines for this connection\n\t\tstartTime := time.Now()\n\t\tgo node.pingLoop(ctx)\n\t\tgo node.healthLoop(ctx, startTime)\n\t\tgo node.readLoop(ctx, errChan)\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// provisionToken provisions a token. Tries the mothership API first,\n// falls back to a synthetic HMAC token.\nfunc provisionToken() (string, error) {\n\t// Parse mothership URL to get HTTP endpoint\n\twsURL, err := url.Parse(*flagMothership)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn \"\", fmt.Errorf(\"invalid mothership URL: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\n\thttpURL := *wsURL\n\tif httpURL.Scheme == \"ws\" {\n\t\thttpURL.Scheme = \"http\"\n\t} else if httpURL.Scheme == \"wss\" {\n\t\thttpURL.Scheme = \"https\"\n\t}\n\n\t// Trim /ws suffix to get base URL\n\tbaseURL := strings.TrimSuffix(httpURL.String(), \"/ws\")\n\tbaseURL = strings.TrimSuffix(baseURL, \"/\")\n\tprovisionURL := baseURL + \"/api/provision\"\n\n\t// Try POST /api/provision with synthetic credentials\n\tbody := strings.NewReader(`{\"mac\":\"AA:BB:CC:00:00:00\"}`)\n\tresp, err := http.Post(provisionURL, \"application/json\", body)\n\tif err == nil && resp.StatusCode == http.StatusOK {\n\t\tvar result map[string]interface{}\n\t\tif json.NewDecoder(resp.Body).Decode(&result) == nil {\n\t\t\t_ = resp.Body.Close()\n\t\t\tif token, ok := result[\"node_token\"].(string); ok && token != \"\" {\n\t\t\t\treturn token, nil\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tif resp != nil {\n\t\t_ = resp.Body.Close()\n\t}\n\n\t// Fallback: generate synthetic token\n\th := hmac.New(sha256.New, []byte(\"sim-install-secret\"))\n\th.Write([]byte(\"sim-node\"))\n\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%064x\", h.Sum(nil)), nil\n}\n\n// closeAllNodes closes all node WebSocket connections\nfunc closeAllNodes(nodes []*VirtualNode) {\n\tfor _, node := range nodes {\n\t\tif node.Conn != nil {\n\t\t\tnode.mu.Lock()\n\t\t\tnode.Conn.WriteMessage(websocket.CloseMessage, //nolint:errcheck\n\t\t\t\twebsocket.FormatCloseMessage(websocket.CloseNormalClosure, \"sim shutdown\"))\n\t\t\tnode.Conn.Close() //nolint:errcheck\n\t\t\tnode.mu.Unlock()\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// macToString converts a 6-byte MAC to colon-separated hex\nfunc macToString(mac [6]byte) string {\n\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%02X:%02X:%02X:%02X:%02X:%02X\",\n\t\tmac[0], mac[1], mac[2], mac[3], mac[4], mac[5])\n}\n\n// pingLoop sends WebSocket pings\nfunc (n *VirtualNode) pingLoop(ctx context.Context) {\n\tticker := time.NewTicker(30 * time.Second)\n\tdefer ticker.Stop()\n\n\tfor {\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\tcase <-ticker.C:\n\t\t\tn.mu.Lock()\n\t\t\terr := n.Conn.WriteMessage(websocket.PingMessage, nil)\n\t\t\tn.mu.Unlock()\n\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM] Node %d ping failed: %v\", n.ID, err)\n\t\t\t\treturn\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// healthLoop sends periodic health messages\nfunc (n *VirtualNode) healthLoop(ctx context.Context, startTime time.Time) {\n\tticker := time.NewTicker(10 * time.Second)\n\tdefer ticker.Stop()\n\n\tfor {\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\tcase <-ticker.C:\n\t\t\thealth := map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\t\"type\":            \"health\",\n\t\t\t\t\"mac\":             macToString(n.MAC),\n\t\t\t\t\"timestamp_ms\":    time.Now().UnixMilli(),\n\t\t\t\t\"free_heap_bytes\": 200000,\n\t\t\t\t\"wifi_rssi_dbm\":   -45,\n\t\t\t\t\"uptime_ms\":       time.Since(startTime).Milliseconds(),\n\t\t\t\t\"csi_rate_hz\":     *flagRate,\n\t\t\t\t\"wifi_channel\":    *flagChannel,\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\thealthBytes, err := json.Marshal(health)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM] Node %d marshal health: %v\", n.ID, err)\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tn.mu.Lock()\n\t\t\terr = n.Conn.WriteMessage(websocket.TextMessage, healthBytes)\n\t\t\tn.mu.Unlock()\n\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM] Node %d send health failed: %v\", n.ID, err)\n\t\t\t\treturn\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// readLoop reads downstream messages from the WebSocket\nfunc (n *VirtualNode) readLoop(ctx context.Context, errChan chan<- error) {\n\tfor {\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tn.mu.Lock()\n\t\tconn := n.Conn\n\t\tn.mu.Unlock()\n\n\t\tif conn == nil {\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tconn.SetReadDeadline(time.Now().Add(60 * time.Second)) //nolint:errcheck\n\t\t_, message, err := conn.ReadMessage()\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tselect {\n\t\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n\t\t\t\treturn\n\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif websocket.IsCloseError(err) {\n\t\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM] Node %d connection closed\", n.ID)\n\t\t\t\treturn\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM] Node %d read error: %v\", n.ID, err)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tvar msg map[string]interface{}\n\t\tif err := json.Unmarshal(message, &msg); err != nil {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tmsgType, ok := msg[\"type\"].(string)\n\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tswitch msgType {\n\t\tcase \"role\":\n\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM] Node %d role update: %v\", n.ID, msg[\"role\"])\n\t\tcase \"config\":\n\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM] Node %d config update: %v\", n.ID, msg)\n\t\tcase \"reject\":\n\t\t\terrChan <- fmt.Errorf(\"node %d rejected: %v\", n.ID, msg[\"reason\"])\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\tcase \"shutdown\":\n\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM] Node %d received shutdown\", n.ID)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// runSimulation runs the main CSI generation loop\nfunc runSimulation(ctx context.Context, nodes []*VirtualNode, walkers []*Walker, space *Space, rng *rand.Rand, csvWriter *CSVWriter, stats *Stats, done chan<- struct{}, scenario *ScenarioConfig) {\n\tdefer close(done)\n\n\tticker := time.NewTicker(time.Duration(1000/(*flagRate)) * time.Millisecond)\n\tdefer ticker.Stop()\n\n\tframeNum := 0\n\tlastBLETime := time.Now()\n\n\t// Initialize fall scenario state\n\tvar fallState *FallScenarioState\n\tif scenario.Type == ScenarioFall || scenario.Type == ScenarioBagOnCouch {\n\t\tif len(walkers) > 0 {\n\t\t\tfallState = &FallScenarioState{\n\t\t\t\tWalker: walkers[0],\n\t\t\t\tState:  \"walking\",\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif scenario.Type == ScenarioBagOnCouch {\n\t\t\t\t// For bag-on-couch, start with a lower position\n\t\t\t\twalkers[0].Position.Z = 1.0\n\t\t\t\twalkers[0].Velocity.Z = -0.2 // Slow descent\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Track scenario timing\n\tscenarioStarted := false\n\n\tfor {\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\tcase <-ticker.C:\n\t\t\t// Handle fall scenario timing\n\t\t\tif fallState != nil && !scenarioStarted && time.Since(scenario.StartedAt) >= scenario.FallParams.TriggerAfter {\n\t\t\t\tif scenario.Type == ScenarioFall {\n\t\t\t\t\tfallState.StartFall(scenario.FallParams)\n\t\t\t\t\tscenarioStarted = true\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t// Update walker positions\n\t\t\tif fallState != nil {\n\t\t\t\tdt := 1.0 / float64(*flagRate)\n\t\t\t\tfallState.UpdateForFallScenario(dt, scenario.FallParams, space, rng)\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\tupdateWalkers(walkers, space, rng)\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t// Write to CSV\n\t\t\tif csvWriter != nil {\n\t\t\t\tcsvWriter.WriteRow(walkers, nodes, walls)\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t// Send CSI frames for each node pair\n\t\t\tfor _, txNode := range nodes {\n\t\t\t\tfor _, rxNode := range nodes {\n\t\t\t\t\tif txNode.ID == rxNode.ID {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\t\tframe := generateCSIFrame(txNode, rxNode, walkers, walls, frameNum, rng)\n\n\t\t\t\t\ttxNode.mu.Lock()\n\t\t\t\t\terr := txNode.Conn.WriteMessage(websocket.BinaryMessage, frame)\n\t\t\t\t\ttxNode.mu.Unlock()\n\n\t\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM] Node %d send CSI failed: %v\", txNode.ID, err)\n\t\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\t\tstats.FramesSent.Add(1)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t// Send BLE messages if enabled\n\t\t\tif *flagBLE && time.Since(lastBLETime) > 5*time.Second {\n\t\t\t\tsendBLEMessages(nodes, walkers)\n\t\t\t\tlastBLETime = time.Now()\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tframeNum++\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// updateWalkers updates walker positions based on their movement type\nfunc updateWalkers(walkers []*Walker, space *Space, rng *rand.Rand) {\n\tdt := 1.0 / float64(*flagRate)\n\n\tfor _, walker := range walkers {\n\t\tswitch walker.Type {\n\t\tcase WalkerTypePathFollow:\n\t\t\tupdatePathWalker(walker, dt)\n\t\tcase WalkerTypeNodeToNode:\n\t\t\tupdateNodeToNodeWalker(walker, dt, space)\n\t\tcase WalkerTypeRandomWalk:\n\t\t\tupdateRandomWalker(walker, dt, space, rng)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// updateRandomWalker implements random walk motion\nfunc updateRandomWalker(walker *Walker, dt float64, space *Space, rng *rand.Rand) {\n\twalker.Position.X += walker.Velocity.X * dt\n\twalker.Position.Y += walker.Velocity.Y * dt\n\n\t// Bounce off walls\n\tmargin := 0.2\n\tif walker.Position.X < margin {\n\t\twalker.Position.X = margin\n\t\twalker.Velocity.X *= -1\n\t}\n\tif walker.Position.X > space.Width-margin {\n\t\twalker.Position.X = space.Width - margin\n\t\twalker.Velocity.X *= -1\n\t}\n\tif walker.Position.Y < margin {\n\t\twalker.Position.Y = margin\n\t\twalker.Velocity.Y *= -1\n\t}\n\tif walker.Position.Y > space.Depth-margin {\n\t\twalker.Position.Y = space.Depth - margin\n\t\twalker.Velocity.Y *= -1\n\t}\n\n\t// Random velocity perturbation\n\tperturbation := 0.1\n\twalker.Velocity.X += (rng.Float64() - 0.5) * perturbation\n\twalker.Velocity.Y += (rng.Float64() - 0.5) * perturbation\n\n\t// Clamp velocity\n\tspeed := walker.Speed * (0.5 + rng.Float64()*0.5)\n\tcurrentSpeed := math.Sqrt(walker.Velocity.X*walker.Velocity.X + walker.Velocity.Y*walker.Velocity.Y)\n\tif currentSpeed > 0 {\n\t\twalker.Velocity.X = (walker.Velocity.X / currentSpeed) * speed\n\t\twalker.Velocity.Y = (walker.Velocity.Y / currentSpeed) * speed\n\t}\n\n\twalker.Position.Z = walker.Height\n}\n\n// updatePathWalker implements path-following motion\nfunc updatePathWalker(walker *Walker, dt float64) {\n\tif len(walker.Path) == 0 {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\ttarget := walker.Path[walker.PathIdx]\n\tdx := target.X - walker.Position.X\n\tdy := target.Y - walker.Position.Y\n\tdz := target.Z - walker.Position.Z\n\tdist := math.Sqrt(dx*dx + dy*dy + dz*dz)\n\n\t// If very close to target, move to next waypoint\n\tif dist < 0.1 {\n\t\twalker.PathIdx = (walker.PathIdx + 1) % len(walker.Path)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Move towards target at constant speed\n\tmoveDist := walker.Speed * dt\n\tif moveDist > dist {\n\t\tmoveDist = dist\n\t}\n\n\tt := moveDist / dist\n\twalker.Position.X += dx * t\n\twalker.Position.Y += dy * t\n\n\t// Update velocity vector for consistency\n\tif dist > 0 {\n\t\twalker.Velocity.X = (dx / dist) * walker.Speed\n\t\twalker.Velocity.Y = (dy / dist) * walker.Speed\n\t\twalker.Velocity.Z = (dz / dist) * walker.Speed\n\t}\n}\n\n// updateNodeToNodeWalker implements traversal between virtual nodes\nfunc updateNodeToNodeWalker(walker *Walker, dt float64, space *Space) {\n\tif len(walker.Nodes) < 2 {\n\t\tupdateRandomWalker(walker, dt, space, rand.New(rand.NewSource(time.Now().UnixNano())))\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\ttargetNode := walker.Nodes[walker.NodeIdx]\n\ttargetPos := targetNode.Position\n\n\tdx := targetPos.X - walker.Position.X\n\tdy := targetPos.Y - walker.Position.Y\n\tdz := targetPos.Z - walker.Position.Z\n\tdist := math.Sqrt(dx*dx + dy*dy + dz*dz)\n\n\t// Check if we've arrived at the target node (horizontal distance)\n\thorizontalDist := math.Sqrt(dx*dx + dy*dy)\n\tif horizontalDist < 0.3 {\n\t\t// Move to next node\n\t\twalker.NodeIdx = (walker.NodeIdx + 1) % len(walker.Nodes)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Move towards target node\n\tmoveDist := walker.Speed * dt\n\tif moveDist > horizontalDist {\n\t\tmoveDist = horizontalDist\n\t}\n\n\tt := moveDist / horizontalDist\n\twalker.Position.X += dx * t\n\twalker.Position.Y += dy * t\n\n\t// Update velocity vector\n\tif horizontalDist > 0 {\n\t\twalker.Velocity.X = (dx / horizontalDist) * walker.Speed\n\t\twalker.Velocity.Y = (dy / horizontalDist) * walker.Speed\n\t\twalker.Velocity.Z = (dz / dist) * walker.Speed\n\t}\n\n\twalker.Position.Z = walker.Height\n}\n\n// sendBLEMessages sends synthetic BLE scan results\nfunc sendBLEMessages(nodes []*VirtualNode, walkers []*Walker) {\n\tfor _, node := range nodes {\n\t\tdevices := make([]map[string]interface{}, 0)\n\n\t\tfor _, walker := range walkers {\n\t\t\tdx := walker.Position.X - node.Position.X\n\t\t\tdy := walker.Position.Y - node.Position.Y\n\t\t\tdz := walker.Position.Z - node.Position.Z\n\t\t\tdist := math.Sqrt(dx*dx + dy*dy + dz*dz)\n\n\t\t\trssi := -50.0 - 20.0*math.Log10(dist/1.0)\n\t\t\tif rssi < -90 {\n\t\t\t\trssi = -90\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tdevices = append(devices, map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\t\"addr\": fmt.Sprintf(\"AA:BB:CC:DD:EE:%02X\", walker.ID),\n\t\t\t\t\"rssi\": int(rssi),\n\t\t\t\t\"name\": fmt.Sprintf(\"sim-person-%d\", walker.ID),\n\t\t\t})\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif len(devices) == 0 {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tbleMsg := map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\t\"type\":         \"ble\",\n\t\t\t\"mac\":          macToString(node.MAC),\n\t\t\t\"timestamp_ms\": time.Now().UnixMilli(),\n\t\t\t\"devices\":      devices,\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tbleBytes, err := json.Marshal(bleMsg)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tlog.Printf(\"[SIM] Node %d marshal BLE: %v\", node.ID, range [-127, 127]\nfunc TestIQClamping(t *testing.T) {\n\trng := rand.New(rand.NewSource(42))\n\n\ttx := &VirtualNode{ID: 0, Position: Point{X: 0, Y: 0, Z: 2}}\n\trx := &VirtualNode{ID: 1, Position: Point{X: 0.1, Y: 0, Z: 2}}\n\twalkers := []*Walker{{ID: 0, Position: Point{X: 0.05, Y: 0, Z: 1.7}}}\n\n\tframe := generateCSIFrame(tx, rx, walkers, nil, 0, rng)\n\n\tfor k := 0; k < 64; k++ {\n\t\toffset := headerSize + k*2\n\t\ti := int8(frame[offset])\n\t\tq := int8(frame[offset+1])\n\n\t\tif i < -127 || i > 127 {\n\t\t\tt.Errorf(\"I value out of range at subcarrier %d: %d\", k, i)\n\t\t}\n\t\tif q < -127 || q > 127 {\n\t\t\tt.Errorf(\"Q value out of range at subcarrier %d: %d\", k, q)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// TestHelloMessageFormat tests that hello message can be parsed \"AA:BB:CC:DD:EE:FF\",\n\t\t\"firmware_version\": \"sim-1.0.0\",\n\t\t\"capabilities\":     []string{\"csi\", \"tx\", \"rx\"},\n\t\t\"chip\":             \"ESP32-S3\",\n\t\t\"flash_mb\":         16,\n\t\t\"uptime_ms\":        1000,\n\t\t\"wifi_rssi\":        -45,\n\t\t\"ip\":               \"127.0.0.1\",\n\t}\n\n\tif hello[\"type\"] != \"hello\" {\n\t\tt.Error(\"Wrong message []struct {\n\t\tname         string\n\t\tblobCount    int\n\t\twalkerCount  int\n\t\texpectedPass bool\n\t}{\n\t\t{\"Exact match\", 1, 1, true},\n\t\t{\"Within tolerance +1\", 2, 1, true},\n\t\t{\"Within tolerance -1\", 0, 1, true},\n\t\t{\"Too many blobs\", 3, 1, false},\n\t\t{\"Multiple walkers exact\", 2, 2, true},\n\t\t{\"Multiple walkers within tolerance\", 3, 2, true},\n\t\t{\"Multiple walkers too few\", 0, 2, false},\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, tt := range tests {\n\t\tt.Run(tt.name, func(t *testing.T) {\n\t\t\ttolerance := 1\n\t\t\tminExpected := tt.walkerCount - {\n\t\t\t\tt.Errorf(\"verifyBlobs(%d walkers, %d blobs) = %v, expected %v\",\n\t\t\t\t\ttt.walkerCount, tt.blobCount, pass, tt.expectedPass)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t})\n\t}\n}\n\n// TestSeedReproducibility tests that the same seed produces identical results\nfunc TestSeedReproducibility(t *testing.T) {\n\tseed := int64(42)\n\n\trng1 := rand.New(rand.NewSource(seed))\n\trng2 := rand.New(rand.NewSource(seed))\n\n\ttx := &VirtualNode{ID: 0, Position: Point{X: 0, Y: 0, Z: 2}}\n\trx := &VirtualNode{ID: 1, Position: Point{X: 5, Y: 0, Z: 2}}\n\twalkers := []*Walker{{ID: 0, Position: Point{X: 2.5, Y: 0, Z: 1.7}}}\n\n\tframe1 := generateCSIFrame(tx, rx, walkers, nil, 0, rng1)\n\tframe2 := generateCSIFrame(tx, rx, walkers, nil, 0, rng2)\n\n\tif len(frame1) != len(frame2) {\n\t\tt.Fatalf(\"Frame lengths differ: %d vs %d\", len(frame1), len(frame2))\n\t}\n\n\tfor i := range frame1 {\n\t\tif frame1[i] != frame2[i] {\n\t\t\tt.Errorf(\"Byte %d differs: %d vs %d\", i, frame1[i], frame2[i])\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// TestSeedReproducibilityWalkerPaths tests that identical seeds produce identical walker trajectories\nfunc TestSeedReproducibilityWalkerPaths(t *testing.T) {\n\tseed := int64(42)\n\tspace := &Space{Width: 5, Depth: 5, Height: 2.5}\n\n\trng1 := rand.New(rand.NewSource(seed))\n\twalkers1 := createWalkers(2, space, rng1)\n\n\trng2 := rand.New(rand.NewSource(seed))\n\twalkers2 := createWalkers(2, space, rng2)\n\n\t// Initial positions should match\n\tfor i := range walkers1 {\n\t\tif walkers1[i].Position != walkers2[i].Position {\n\t\t\tt.Errorf(\"Initial position mismatch for walker %d: %v vs %v\",\n\t\t\t\ti, walkers1[i].Position, walkers2[i].Position)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Run 100 update steps and verify positions still match\n\tfor step := 0; step < 100; step++ {\n\t\trng1 = rand.New(rand.NewSource(seed))\n\t\trng2 = rand.New(rand.NewSource(seed))\n\t\t// Reset walkers to get fresh RNG sequence\n\t\twalkers1 = createWalkers(2, space, rng1)\n\t\twalkers2 = createWalkers(2, space, rng2)\n\n\t\t// Apply same number of updates\n\t\tfor s := 0; s <= step; s++ {\n\t\t\tupdateWalkers(walkers1, space, rng1)\n\t\t\tupdateWalkers(walkers2, space, rng2)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tfor i := range walkers1 {\n\t\t\tif walkers1[i].Position != walkers2[i].Position {\n\t\t\t\tt.Errorf(\"Position mismatch at step %d walker %d: %v vs %v\",\n\t\t\t\t\tstep, i, walkers1[i].Position, walkers2[i].Position)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// TestParseSpace tests space dimension parsing\nfunc TestParseSpace(t *testing.T) filepath.Join(tmpDir, \"test_output.csv\")\n\n\tcsvWriter, err := NewCSVWriter(csvPath)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tt.Fatalf(\"Failed to create CSV writer: %v\", err)\n\t}\n\n\twalkers := []*Walker{\n\t\t{ID: 0, Position: Point{X: 2.5, Y: 1.5, Z: 1.7}, Velocity: Point{X: 0.5, Y: 0.3, Z: 0}},\n\t}\n\tnodes := []*VirtualNode{\n\t\t{ID: 0, MAC: generateMAC(0), Position: Point{X: 0, Y: 0, Z: 2}},\n\t\t{ID: 1, MAC: generateMAC(1), Position: Point{X: 5, Y: 0, Z: 2}},\n\t}\n\n\tcsvWriter.WriteRow(walkers, nodes, nil)\n\tcsvWriter.Close() //nolint:errcheck\n\n\t// Read back and verify\n\tfile, err := os.Open(csvPath)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tt.Fatalf(\"Failed to open CSV: %v\", err)\n\t}\n\tdefer func() { _ = file.Close() }()\n\n\treader := csv.NewReader(file)\n\trecords, err := reader.ReadAll()\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tt.Fatalf(\"Failed to read CSV: %v\", err)\n\t}\n\n\t// Check header\n\texpectedHeaders := []string{\"timestamp_ms\", \"walker_id\", \"x\", \"y\", \"z\", \"vx\", \"vy\", \"vz\", \"link_id\", \"delta_rms\"}\n\tif len(records) == 0 {\n\t\tt.Fatal(\"CSV is empty\")\n\t}\n\tfor i, h := range expectedHeaders {\n\t\tif i >= len(records[0]) {\n\t\t\tt.Errorf(\"Missing header column %d: expected %s\", i, h)\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\tif records[0][i] != h {\n\t\t\tt.Errorf(\"Header[%d] = %q, want %q\", i, records[0][i], h)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Should have header + 1 position row + 1 link row (1 unique link pair for 2 nodes)\n\t// With 2 nodes, there's 1 unique pair (0,1), so 1 position row + 1 deltaRMS row = 2 data rows\n\tif len(records) < 3 {\n\t\tt.Errorf(\"Expected at least 3 rows (header + position + deltaRMS), got %d\", len(records))\n\t}\n\n\t// Verify position row has walker data\n\tposRow := \"2.500\")\n\t}\n\n\t// Verify deltaRMS row has link data\n\tdeltaRow := records[2]\n\tif deltaRow[8] == \"\" {\n\t\tt.Error(\"Expected link_id in deltaRMS row but got empty\")\n\t}\n\tif deltaRow[9] == \"\" {\n\t\tt.Error(\"Expected delta_rms value but got empty\")\n\t}\n\tif !strings.Contains(deltaRow[8], \":\") {\n\t\tt.Errorf(\"link_id should contain MAC separator ':', got %q\", deltaRow[8])\n\t}\n}\n\n// TestDeltaRMSComputation tests that deltaRMS values are physically plausible\nfunc TestDeltaRMSComputation(t *testing.T) {\n\ttx := Point{X: 0, Y: 0, Z: 2}\n\trx := Point{X: Depth: 5, Height: 2.5}\n\trng := rand.New(rand.NewSource(42))\n\n\twalker := &Walker{\n\t\tID:       0,\n\t\tType:     WalkerTypeRandomWalk,\n\t\tPosition: Point{X: 0.1, Y: 2.5, Z: 1.7}, // Near left wall\n\t\tVelocity: Point{X: -1.0, Y: 0, Z: 0},     // Moving left\n\t\tSpeed:    1.0,\n\t\tHeight:   1.7,\n\t}\n\n\t// Run several updates — should bounce off left wall\n\tfor i := 0; i < 10; i++ {\n\t\tupdateWalkers([]*Walker{walker}, space, rng)\n\t}\n\n\t// Walker should not be outside room bounds\n\tif walker.Position.X < 0 || walker.Position.X > space.Width {\n\t\tt.Errorf(\"Walker X=%v
