space.Depth)\n\t}\n}\n\n// TestPathFollowing tests that walkers follow a predefined path\nfunc TestPathFollowing(t *testing.T) {\n\tspace := &Space{Width: 5, Depth: 5, Height: 2.5}\n\n\t// Create a rectangular path\n\tpath := []Point{\n\t\t{X: 0.5, Y: 0.5, Z: 1.7},\n\t\t{X: 4.5, Y: 0.5, Z: 1.7},\n\t\t{X: 4.5, Y: 4.5, Z: 1.7},\n\t\t{X: 0.5, Y: 4.5, Z: 1.7},\n\t}\n\n\twalker := &Walker{\n\t\tID:       0,\n\t\tType:     WalkerTypePathFollow,\n\t\tPath:     path,\n\t\tPathIdx:  0,\n\t\tSpeed:    1.0,\n\t\tHeight:   1.7,\n\t\tPosition: path[0], // Initialize at first waypoint\n\t}\n\n\t// Run updates - should move along path\n\tfor i := 0; i < 100; i++ {\n\t\tupdatePathWalker(walker, 0.1)\n\t}\n\n\t// Walker should have moved from starting position\n\tif walker.Position == path[0] {\n\t\tt.Error(\"Walker should have moved from starting position\")\n\t}\n\n\t// Walker should remain within room bounds\n\tif walker.Position.X < 0 || walker.Position.X > space.Width %v]\", walker.Position.Y, space.Depth)\n\t}\n}\n\n// TestNodeToNodeTraversal tests node-to-node walker movement\nfunc TestNodeToNodeTraversal(t *testing.T) {\n\tspace := &Space{Width: 5, Depth: 5, Height: 2.5}\n\n\tnodes := []*VirtualNode{\n\t\t{ID: 0, Position: Point{X: 0.5, Y: 0.5, Z: 2.0}},\n\t\t{ID: 1, Position: Point{X: 4.5, Y: 0.5, Z: 2.0}},\n\t\t{ID: 2, Position: Point{X: 2.5, Y: 4.5, Z: 2.0}},\n\t}\n\n\twalker := &Walker{\n\t\tID:       0,\n\t\tType:     WalkerTypeNodeToNode,\n\t\tNodes:    nodes,\n\t\tNodeIdx:  1, // Target is second node\n\t\tSpeed:    1.0,\n\t\tHeight:   1.7,\n\t\tPosition: nodes[0].Position, // Initialize at first node\n\t}\n\n\t// Move towards second node\n\tfor i := 0; i < 100; i++ {\n\t\tupdateNodeToNodeWalker(walker, 0.1, space)\n\t\t// Break if we've moved to the next node\n\t\tif walker.NodeIdx != 1 {\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Walker should have progressed toward the target\n\tdistToTarget := math.Sqrt(\n\t\tmath.Pow(walker.Position.X-nodes[1].Position.X, 2) +\n\t\t\tmath.Pow(walker.Position.Y-nodes[1].Position.Y, 2))\n\tif distToTarget > 1.0 {\n\t\tt.Errorf(\"Walker should be closer to target; distance=%v\", distToTarget)\n\t}\n}\n\n// TestPathFileLoading tests loading paths from JSON file\nfunc TestPathFileLoading(t *testing.T) {\n\ttmpDir := t.TempDir()\n\tpathFile := 1.7},\n\t\t\t\t{X: 1, Y: 1, Z: 1.7},\n\t\t\t\t{X: 0, Y: 1, Z: 1.7},\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t},\n\t}\n\n\tdata, err := json.Marshal(paths)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tt.Fatalf(\"Failed to marshal paths: %v\", `--height` | float64 | `2.5` | Space height in meters |\n33\t| `--space` | string | `\"\"` | Space dimensions as \"WxDxH\" (overrides --width/--depth/--height) |\n34\t| `--show-frame-rate` | bool | `true` | Show per-second frame counts to stdout |\n35\t| `--verbose` | bool | `false` | Enable verbose logging |\n36\t\n37\t### Examples\n38\t\n39\t**Basic simulation (4 nodes, 1 walker, 30 CSI binary frames matching the Spaxel specification:\n72\t\n73\t```\n74\tHeader (24 bytes):\n75\t  node_mac:     6 bytes  — source node MAC\n76\t  peer_mac:     6 bytes  — transmitting peer MAC\n77\t  timestamp_us: 8 bytes  — uint64, microseconds since node boot\n78\t  rssi:         1 byte   — int8, dBm\n79\t  noise_floor:  1 byte   — int8, dBm\n80\t  channel:      1 byte   — uint8, WiFi channel\n81\t  n_sub:        1 byte   — uint8, subcarrier count\n82\t\n83\tPayload (n_sub × 2 bytes):\n84\t  Per subcarrier: int8 I, int8 Q\n85\t```\n86\t\n87\t## Simulation Model\n88\t\n89\t### Virtual Nodes\n90\t- Positioned at corners and edges of the defined space\n91\t- Mixed heights (high at 80% of room height, low at 30%)\n92\t- MAC addresses: `AA:BB:CC:DD:E0:00` through `AA:BB:CC:DD:E0:0N`\n93\t\n94\t### Walkers\n95\t- Start at center of room (average person height: 1.7m)\n96\t- Random walk with Gaussian velocity updates\n97\t- Bounce off walls\n98\t- BLE address: `11:22:33:44:55:00` through `11:22:33:44:55:0N`\n99\t\n100\t### Signal Model\n101\t- **Path loss:** Free space path loss model (PL(d) = PL₀ + 10·n·log₁₀(d/d₀))\n102\t  - PL₀ = 40 dB at d₀ = 1m\n103\t  - n = 2.0 (free space)\n104\t- **Fresnel modulation:** Amplitude increases when walker is in Fresnel zones\n105\t  - Zone 1: maximum modulation\n106\t  - Zone 5+: no modulation\n107\t- **Noise:** Gaussian noise added to I/Q values\n108\t\n109\t## Integration Testing\n110\t\n111\tThe simulator is designed for integration testing:\n112\t\n113\t```bash\n114\t# Start mothership\n115\tdocker run -d The simulator opens WebSocket connections as virtual nodes and sends synthetic CSI binary frames.\n\n## Building\n\n```bash\ncd mothership\ngo build -o spaxel-sim ./cmd/sim\n```\n\n## Usage\n\n```bash\nspaxel-sim [flags]\n```\n\n### Flags\n\n| Flag | Type | Default | Description |\n|------|------|---------|-------------|\n| `--mothership` | string | `ws://localhost:8080/ws/node` | Mothership WebSocket URL |\n| `--token` | string | `\"\"` | Node authentication token (X-Spaxel-Token header) |\n| `--nodes` | int | `4` | Number of virtual nodes to simulate |\n| `--walkers` | int | `1` | Number of walking persons to simulate |\n| `--rate` | int | `20` | CSI packet rate in Hz per node |\n| `--duration` | duration | `30s` | Simulation duration (0 = run forever) |\n| `--ble` | bool | `false` | Also send simulated BLE advertisements |\n| `--seed` | int64 | `42` | Random seed for reproducible runs |\n| `--width` | float64 | `6.0` | Space width in meters |\n| `--depth` | float64 | `5.0` | Space depth in meters |\n| `--height` | float64 | `2.5` | Space height in meters |\n| `--space` | string | `\"\"` | Space dimensions as \"WxDxH\" (overrides --width/--depth/--height) |\n| `--show-frame-rate` | bool | `true` | Show per-second frame counts to stdout |\n| `--verbose` | bool | `false` | Enable verbose logging |\n\n### Examples\n\n**Basic simulation (4 nodes, 1 walker, 30 seconds):**\n```bash\nspaxel-sim --mothership ws://localhost:8080/ws/node --nodes 4 --walkers 1 --duration 30s\n```\n\n**With authentication:**\n```bash\nspaxel-sim --mothership ws://localhost:8080/ws/node --token <your-token> --nodes 4\n```\n\n**Custom space dimensions:**\n```bash\nspaxel-sim --space \"10x8x3.0\" --nodes 6 --walkers 2\n```\n\n**With BLE advertisements:**\n```bash\nspaxel-sim --ble --walkers 2\n```\n\n**Reproducible run (fixed seed):**\n```bash\nspaxel-sim --seed 12345 --duration 60s\n```\n\n**Run indefinitely (for manual testing):**\n```bash\nspaxel-sim --duration 0\n```\n\n## CSI Frame Format\n\nThe simulator generates valid CSI binary frames matching the Spaxel specification:\n\n```\nHeader (24 bytes):\n  node_mac:     6 bytes  — source node MAC\n  peer_mac:     6 bytes  — transmitting peer MAC\n  timestamp_us: 8 bytes  — uint64, microseconds since node boot\n  rssi:         1 byte   — int8, dBm\n  noise_floor:  1 byte   — int8, dBm\n  channel:      1 byte   — uint8, WiFi channel\n  n_sub:        1 byte   — uint8, subcarrier count\n\nPayload (n_sub × 2 bytes):\n  Per subcarrier: int8 I, int8 Q\n```\n\n## Simulation Model\n\n### Virtual Nodes\n- Positioned at corners and edges of the defined space\n- Mixed heights (high at 80% of room height, low at 30%)\n- MAC addresses: `AA:BB:CC:DD:E0:00` through `AA:BB:CC:DD:E0:0N`\n\n### Walkers\n- Start at center of room (average person height: 1.7m)\n- Random walk with Gaussian velocity updates\n- Bounce off walls\n- BLE address: `11:22:33:44:55:00` through `11:22:33:44:55:0N`\n\n### Signal Model\n- **Path loss:** Free space path loss model (PL(d) = PL₀ + 10·n·log₁₀(d/d₀))\n  - PL₀ = 40 dB at d₀ = 1m\n  - n = 2.0 (free space)\n- **Fresnel modulation:** Amplitude increases when walker is in Fresnel zones\n  - Zone 1: maximum modulation\n  - Zone 5+: no modulation\n- **Noise:** Gaussian noise added to I/Q values\n\n## Integration Testing\n\nThe simulator is designed for integration testing:\n\n```bash\n# Start mothership\ndocker run -d -p 8080:8080 --name spaxel-test ghcr.io/spaxel/spaxel:latest\n\n# Run simulator for 30 seconds\nspaxel-sim --mothership ws://localhost:8080/ws/node --nodes 4 --walkers 1 --duration 30s\n\n# Check blob count (should be > 0 if detection is working)\ncurl -s http://localhost:8080/api/blobs | jq '. | length > 0'\n```\n\n## Output\n\nThe simulator logs:\n- Connection status\n- Per-second frame rates (if `--show-frame-rate`)\n- Final statistics on completion\n- Errors (authentication failures, WebSocket errors, etc.)\n\nExample output:\n```\n[INFO] CSI Simulator starting\n[INFO] Configuration: nodes=4, walkers=1, rate=20 Hz, duration=30s\n[INFO] Space: 6.0x5.0x2.5 m\n[INFO] Connecting to: ws://localhost:8080/ws/node\n[INFO] Node AA:BB:CC:DD:E0:00 connected to mothership\n[STATS] Node AA:BB:CC:DD:E0:00: 20 frames/s\n[STATS] Node AA:BB:CC:DD:E0:00: 20 frames/s\n[INFO] Simulation completed successfully\n[STATS] Node AA:BB:CC:DD:E0:00: sent 600 frames\n```\n\n## Authentication\n\nWhen the mothership requires authentication (SPAXEL_INSTALL_SECRET is set), you must provide a valid node token.
